<title>Identitat d'Euler</title>
<math>e^{i \cdot \pi} + 1 = 0</math>
<math>e^{x+i \cdot y} = e^x \cdot (\cos y + i \cdot \sin y )</math>
<math>e^{ix} = \cos x +  i\sin x \,\!</math>
<math>e^{i \pi} = \cos \pi +  i\sin \pi\,\!</math>
<math>\cos \pi = -1  \, \! </math>
<math>\sin \pi = 0\,\!</math>
<math>e^{i \pi} = -1 + 0 i\,\!</math>
<math>e^{i \pi} +1 = 0\,\!</math>

<title>Evoluta</title>
<math>\mathbf{T}(s) = \gamma'(s)</math>
<math>\mathbf{T}'(s) = k(s)\mathbf{N}(s)</math>
<math>R(s) = \frac{1}{k(s)}.</math>
<math>E(s) = \gamma(s) + R(s)\mathbf{N}(s) = \gamma(s) + \frac{1}{k(s)}\mathbf{N}(s).</math>
<math>(X,Y) = (x,y) + R \mathbf{N} = (x-R\sin\varphi,y+R\cos\varphi)</math>
<math>(\cos \varphi, \sin \varphi) = \frac{(x', y')}{(x'^2+y'^2)^{1/2}}</math>
<math>R = 1/k = \frac{(x'^2+y'^2)^{3/2}}{x'y''-x''y'},</math>
<math>X[x,y]= x-y'\frac{x'^2+y'^2}{x'y''-x''y'}</math>
<math>Y[x,y]= y+x'\frac{x'^2+y'^2}{x'y''-x''y'}</math>
<math>\int_{s_1}^{s_2}\left|\frac{dR}{ds}\right| ds = |R(s_2)-R(s_1)|.</math>
<math>\frac{d\sigma}{ds} = \left|\frac{dR}{ds}\right|.</math>
<math>E(s) = \gamma(s) + R(s)\mathbf{N}(s)</math>
<math>E'(s) = \gamma'(s) +R'(s)\mathbf{N}(s) - \mathbf{T}(s) = R'(s)\mathbf{N}(s)</math>
<math>\frac{dE}{ds} = \frac{dR}{ds}\mathbf{N}\left ( s \right ) </math>
<math>
\frac{dE}{d\sigma} = \left.\frac{dE}{ds}\right/\frac{d\sigma}{ds} = \pm\mathbf{N}</math>
<math>\frac{d^2E}{d\sigma^2} = \pm\left.\frac{d\mathbf{N}}{ds}\right/\frac{d\sigma}{ds} = -\frac{1}{RR'}\frac{dE}{d\sigma}.</math>
<math>k_E = -\frac{1}{RR'}</math>
<math>(X, Y)= \left(-y'\frac{x'^2+y'^2}{x'y''-x''y'}, x'\frac{x'^2+y'^2}{x'y''-x''y'}\right).</math>

<title>Relació d'Einstein (Teoria cinètica)</title>
<math> D = \mu \, k_B T </math>
<math> D = {{\mu_q \, k_B T}\over{q}}</math>
<math> D=\frac{k_B T}{6\pi\,\eta\,r} </math>
<math> D = \frac{\mu_q \, k_B T}{q} </math>
<math>\gamma = \zeta / m</math>
<math>\zeta = 6 \pi \, \eta \, r,</math>
<math>D = \frac{k_\mathrm{B} T}{6\pi\,\eta\,r}</math>
<math>\zeta_\mathrm{r} = 8 \pi \eta r^3</math>
<math>D_\mathrm{r} = \frac{k_\mathrm{B} T}{8\pi\,\eta\,r^3}</math>
<math> D = \frac{\mu_q \, p}{q  \frac{dp}{d\eta} } </math>
<math>F=-dU/dx</math>
<math>v=\mu F</math>
<math>J_\mathrm{drift}(x) = \mu \, F(x) \, \rho(x) = -\rho(x) \mu \frac{dU}{dx}</math>
<math>J_\mathrm{diffusion} (x)=-D \frac{d\rho}{dx}</math>
<math>0 = J_\mathrm{drift} + J_\mathrm{diffusion} = -\rho(x) \mu \frac{dU}{dx} - D \frac{d\rho}{dx} </math>
<math>\rho(x) = A e^{-U/ (k_B T)}</math>
<math> \frac{d\rho}{dx} = -\frac{1}{k_B T}\frac{dU}{dx} \rho(x).</math>
<math>0 = J_\mathrm{drift} + J_\mathrm{diffusion} = -\rho(x) \mu \frac{dU}{dx} + \frac{D}{k_B T} \frac{dU}{dx}\rho(x) = -\rho(x)\frac{dU}{dx} \left(\mu - \frac{D}{k_B T} \right)</math>
<math>\mu=\frac{D}{k_B T}.</math>

<title>Lema de Jordan</title>
<math>C_R=\{z : z=R \!\cdot\! e^{i \theta}, \theta\in [0,\pi]\}</math>
<math>f(z)=e^{iaz} g(z)\,,\quad z\in C_R,</math>
<math>M_R:=\max_{\theta\in [0,\pi]} \bigl|g \bigl(R \!\cdot\! e^{i \theta}\bigr)\bigr| \to 0\quad \mbox{quan } R \to \infty\,,\qquad(*)</math>
<math>\lim_{R \to \infty} \int_{C_R} f(z)\, dz = 0.</math>
<math>\oint_{C} f(z)\, dz = \int_{C_1}f(z)\,dz + \int_{C_2} f(z)\,dz\,.</math>
<math>\int_{C_2} f(z)\,dz = \int_{-R}^{R} f(x)\,dx\,.</math>
<math>\oint_{C} f(z)\, dz = 2\pi i \sum_{k=1}^n \operatorname{Res}(f, z_k)\,,</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^{\infty} f(x)\,dx = 2\pi i \sum_{k=1}^n \operatorname{Res}(f, z_k)\,.</math>
<math>f(z)=\frac{e^{iz}}{1+z^2},\qquad z\in{\mathbb C}\setminus\{i,-i\},</math>
<math>M_R=\max_{\theta\in[0,\pi]}\frac1{|1+R^2e^{2i\theta}|}=\frac1{R^2-1}\,,</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{e^{ix}}{1+x^2}\,dx=2\pi i\,\operatorname{Res}(f,i)\,.</math>
<math>\operatorname{Res}(f,i)=\lim_{z\to i}(z-i)f(z)
=\lim_{z\to i}\frac{e^{iz}}{z+i}=\frac{e^{-1}}{2i}</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{\cos x}{1+x^2}\,dx=\operatorname{Re}\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{e^{ix}}{1+x^2}\,dx=\frac{\pi}{e}\,.</math>
<math>\begin{align}
\int_{C_R} f(z)\, dz
&amp;=\int_0^\pi g(R \!\cdot\! e^{i\theta})\,e^{iaR(\cos\theta+i \sin\theta)}\,i R \!\cdot\! e^{i\theta}\,d\theta\\
&amp;=R\int_0^\pi g(R \!\cdot\! e^{i\theta})\,e^{aR(i\cos\theta-\sin\theta)}\,ie^{i\theta}\,d\theta\,.
\end{align}</math>
<math>\begin{align}
I_R:=\biggl|\int_{C_R} f(z)\, dz\biggr|
&amp;\le R\int_0^\pi\bigl|g(R \!\cdot\! e^{i\theta})\,e^{aR(i\cos\theta-\sin\theta)}\,ie^{i\theta} \bigr|\,d\theta\\
&amp;=R\int_0^\pi \bigl|g(R \!\cdot\! e^{i\theta})\bigr|\,e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta\,.
\end{align}</math>
<math> I_R \le RM_R\int_0^\pi e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta = 2RM_R\int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta\,.</math>
<math>I_R
\le 2RM_R \int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-2aR\theta/\pi}\,d\theta
=\frac{\pi}{a} (1-e^{-a R}) M_R\le\frac\pi{a}M_R\,.</math>

<math>\left(\!\!{n \choose k}\!\!\right) = {n + k -1 \choose k} = \frac{ \left( n + k -1 \right)! }{{\left( n-1 \right)! \cdot k!} }</math>
<math>\tfrac{n!}{(n-k)!} = k!\,\tbinom{n}{k}</math>
<math>\left(\!\!\tbinom{n}{k}\!\!\right)=\tbinom{k+n-1}{n-1}</math>
<math>\left(\!\!\tbinom{n}{k-n}\!\!\right)=\tbinom{k-1}{n-1}</math>
<math>\sum_{r=0}^{n}(-1)^{r}\tbinom{n}{r}\left(\!\!\tbinom{n}{k-rc}\!\!\right)</math>
<math>\sum_{r=0}^{n}(-1)^{r}\tbinom{n}{r}\left(\!\!\tbinom{n}{k-rc}\!\!\right)^{+}</math>
<math>\sum_{r=0}^{n}S_{k,r}</math>
<math>\begin{array}{lll} 1 &amp;: &amp;k\leq n \\ 0 &amp;: &amp;k&gt;n \end{array}</math>

<math>\sum_{i\in\Z} a_iX^i\, \cdot \, \sum_{j\in\Z} b_jX^j = \sum_{k\in\Z} \left(\sum_{i,j: i + j = k} a_i b_j\right)X^k</math>

<title>Standardisierung (Statistik)</title>
<math>\operatorname{E}(X) = \mu</math>
<math>\operatorname{Var}(X) = \sigma^2</math>
<math>\sigma = \sqrt{\operatorname{Var}(X)}</math>
<math>Z=\frac{X-\mu}{\sigma}</math>
<math>\operatorname{E}(Z)= \operatorname{E}\left(\frac{X-\mu}{\sigma}\right)=\frac{1}{\sigma} \left( \operatorname{E}(X) - \mu\right) = 0</math>
<math>\operatorname{Var}(Z)= \operatorname{Var}\left(\frac{X-\mu}{\sigma}\right)=\operatorname{Var}\left(\frac{X}{\sigma}\right) =\frac{1}{\sigma^2} \operatorname{Var}(X) = 1</math>
<math>Z = \frac{X - \mu}{\sigma}</math>

= \frac{1}{2\pi i} \int_{c-i\infty}^{c+i\infty} 
\frac{\Gamma(1+\delta)\Gamma(s)}{\Gamma(1+\delta+s)} \zeta(s) \lambda^s \, ds
= \frac{\lambda}{1+\delta} + \sum_n b_n \lambda^{-n}.
</math>

\sum_{n\le \lambda} \left(1-\frac{n}{\lambda}\right)^\delta \Lambda(n)

= \frac{\lambda}{1+\delta} + 
\sum_\rho \frac {\Gamma(1+\delta)\Gamma(\rho)}{\Gamma(1+\delta+\rho)}

<title>Power (physics)</title>
<math>\text{power}=\frac{\text{work}}{\text{time}}</math>
<math>P =\frac{dW}{dt}</math>
<math>W = \mathbf{F} \cdot \mathbf{x}</math>
<math>P =\frac{dW}{dt}= \frac{d}{dt}\left(\mathbf{F}\cdot\mathbf{x}\right)= \mathbf{F}\cdot \frac{d\mathbf{x}}{dt} = \mathbf{F} \cdot \mathbf {v}</math>
<math>
P_\mathrm{avg} = \frac{\Delta W}{\Delta t}\,.
</math>
<math>
P = \lim _{\Delta t\rightarrow 0} P_\mathrm{avg} = \lim _{\Delta t\rightarrow 0} \frac{\Delta W}{\Delta t} =  \frac{\mathrm{d}W}{\mathrm{d}t}\,.
</math>
<math>
W = Pt\,.
</math>
<math>W_C = \int_{C}\mathbf{F}\cdot \mathbf{v}\,\mathrm{d}t =\int_{C} \mathbf{F} \cdot \mathrm{d}\mathbf{x},</math>
<math>W_C = U(B)-U(A),</math>
<math>P(t) = \frac{\mathrm{d}W}{\mathrm{d}t}=\mathbf{F}\cdot \mathbf{v}=-\frac{\mathrm{d}U}{\mathrm{d}t}.</math>
<math>P(t) = F\cdot v.</math>
<math>P(t) = \boldsymbol{\tau} \cdot \boldsymbol{\omega}, \,</math>
<math> P(t) = pQ, \!</math>
<math>P = F_B v_B = F_A v_A, \!</math>
<math> \mathrm{MA} = \frac{F_B}{F_A} = \frac{v_A}{v_B}. </math>
<math>P = T_A \omega_A = T_B \omega_B, \!</math>
<math> \mathrm{MA} = \frac{T_B}{T_A} = \frac{\omega_A}{\omega_B}.</math>
<math>
P(t) = I(t) \cdot V(t) \,
</math>
<math>
P=I \cdot V = I^2 \cdot R = \frac{V^2}{R} \,
</math>
<math>
R = \frac{V}{I} \,
</math>
<math>p(t) = |s(t)|^2</math>
<math>
P_0 = \max [p(t)]
</math>
<math>
\epsilon_\mathrm{pulse} = \int_{0}^{T}p(t) \mathrm{d}t \,
</math>
<math>
P_\mathrm{avg} = \frac{1}{T} \int_{0}^{T}p(t) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{\epsilon_\mathrm{pulse}}{T} \,
</math>
<math>P_0\tau = \epsilon_\mathrm{pulse}</math>
<math>
\frac{P_\mathrm{avg}}{P_0} = \frac{\tau}{T} \,
</math>
<math>P(r) = I(4\pi r^2) </math>

<title>Casorati–Weierstrass theorem</title>
<math>a=\infty</math>

<math>\left| f(z) \right| = \left| e^{\frac{1}{r}\cos \theta} \right| \left| e^{-\frac{1}{r}i \sin(\theta)} \right | =e^{\frac{1}{r}\cos \theta}.</math>

<title>Inelastic collision</title>
<math>v_a=\frac{C_R m_b (u_b - u_a) + m_a u_a + m_b u_b} {m_a+m_b}</math>
<math>v_b=\frac{C_R m_a (u_a - u_b) + m_a u_a + m_b u_b} {m_a+m_b}</math>
<math>v_a=-C_R u_a</math>
<math>v_b=-C_R u_b</math>

<math>m_a u_a + m_b u_b = \left( m_a + m_b \right)  v \,</math>

<title>Goodstein's theorem</title>

<title>Liouville–Neumann series</title>
<math>\phi\left(x\right) = \sum^\infty_{n=0} \lambda^n \phi_n \left(x\right)</math>
<math>f(t)= \phi(t) - \lambda \int_a^bK(t,s)\phi(s)\,ds.</math>
<math>K_n\left(x,z\right) = \int\int\cdots\int K\left(x,y_1\right)K\left(y_1,y_2\right) \cdots K\left(y_{n-1}, z\right) dy_1 dy_2 \cdots dy_{n-1}</math>
<math>\phi_n\left(x\right) = \int K_n\left(x,z\right)f\left(z\right)dz</math>
<math>\phi_0\left(x\right) = f\left(x\right)~,</math>
<math>R\left(x, z;\lambda\right) = \sum^\infty_{n=0} \lambda^n K_{n} \left(x, z\right).
</math>
<math>\phi\left(x\right) = \int R\left( x, z;\lambda\right) f\left(z\right)dz.</math>

&amp; \int_{\mathbb{R}^n} e^{- x^T A x + v^T x}  \left( a^T x \right) \, dx = (a^T u) \cdot \mathcal{M}\;,\text{ where } u = \frac{1}{2} A^{- 1} v \;. \\[6pt]

= {} &amp; \left( 2 \operatorname{tr} (A' \Lambda A B^{- 1}) + 4 u^T A' \Lambda A u - 2 u^T (A' \Lambda s + A \Lambda s') + s'^T \Lambda s \right) \cdot \mathcal{M}\;,\\[6pt]

</math>

<title>Fixed-rate mortgage</title>
<math>c = {r\over{1-(1+r)^{-N}}}P_0</math>
<math>P_0=200000</math>
<math>r=6.5/100/12</math>
<math>N=30\cdot 12=360</math>
<math>c=\$1264.14</math>
<math>{}=1264.14</math>
<math>P_1 = P_0+P_0*r-c </math>
<math>P_1 = P_0(1+r)-c</math>
<math>P_2 = P_1(1+r)-c</math>
<math>P_2 = (P_0(1+r)-c)(1+r)-c</math>
<math>P_2 = P_0(1+r)^2- c(1+r)- c</math>
<math>P_3 = P_2(1+r) - c</math>
<math>P_3 = (P_0(1+r)^2- c(1+r)- c)(1+r) - c</math>
<math>P_3 = P_0(1+r)^3- c(1+r)^2- c(1+r) - c</math>
<math>P_N = P_{N-1}(1+r) - c</math>
<math>P_N = P_0(1+r)^N - c(1+r)^{N-1} - c(1+r)^{N-2} .... - c</math>
<math>P_N = P_0(1+r)^N - c ((1+r)^{N-1} + (1+r)^{N-2} .... + 1)</math>
<math>P_N = P_0(1+r)^N - c (S)</math>
<math>S = (1+r)^{N-1} + (1+r)^{N-2} .... + 1</math>
<math>S(1+r) = (1+r)^N + (1+r)^{N-1} .... + (1+r)</math>
<math>S(1+r)-S = (1+r)^N - 1</math>
<math>S((1+r)-1) = (1+r)^N - 1</math>
<math>S(r) = (1+r)^N - 1</math>
<math>S = {{(1+r)^N - 1}\over r}</math>
<math>P_N = P_0(1+r)^N - c {{(1+r)^N - 1}\over r}</math>
<math>0 = P_0(1+r)^N - c {{(1+r)^N - 1}\over r}</math>
<math>c = {{r(1+r)^N} \over {(1+r)^N-1}} P_0</math>
<math>c = {r \over {1-(1+r)^{-N}}} P_0</math>

<title>Exponential integral</title>
<math> \operatorname{Ei}(x)=-\int_{-x}^{\infty}\frac{e^{-t}}t\,dt.\,</math>
<math>E_1(z) = \int_z^\infty \frac{e^{-t}}{t}\,  dt,\qquad|{\rm Arg}(z)|&lt;\pi</math>
<math>-E_1(x) = \operatorname{Ei}(-x)</math>
<math>E_1(z) = \int_1^\infty \frac{e^{-tz}}{t}\, dt = \int_0^1 \frac{e^{-z/u}}{u}\, du ,\qquad \Re(z) \ge 0.</math>
<math>\lim_{\delta\to0+} E_1(-x \pm i\delta) = -\operatorname{Ei}(x) \mp i\pi,\qquad x&gt;0.</math>
<math>E_1(z) =-\gamma-\ln z-\sum_{k=1}^{\infty}\frac{(-z)^k}{k\; k!} \qquad (|\operatorname{Arg}(z)| &lt; \pi)</math>
<math>{\rm Ei} (x) = \gamma + \ln x + \exp{(x/2)} \sum_{n=1}^\infty \frac{ (-1)^{n-1} x^n} {n! \, 2^{n-1}} \sum_{k=0}^{\lfloor (n-1)/2 \rfloor} \frac{1}{2k+1}</math>
<math>E_1(z)=\frac{\exp(-z)} z \sum_{n=0}^{N-1} \frac{n!}{(-z)^n}
</math>
<math>N=1</math>
<math>N=5</math>
<math>
\frac 1 2 e^{-x}\,\ln\!\left( 1+\frac 2 x \right)
&lt; E_1(x) &lt; e^{-x}\,\ln\!\left( 1+\frac 1 x \right)
\qquad x&gt;0
</math>
<math>
\operatorname{Ein}(z)
= \int_0^z (1-e^{-t})\frac{dt}{t}
= \sum_{k=1}^\infty \frac{(-1)^{k+1}z^k}{k\; k!}
</math>
<math>
E_1(z) \,=\, -\gamma-\ln z + {\rm Ein}(z)
\qquad |\operatorname{Arg}(z)| &lt; \pi
</math>
<math>\operatorname{Ei}(x) \,=\, \gamma+\ln x - \operatorname{Ein}(-x)
\qquad x&gt;0
</math>
<math>z\frac{d^2w}{dz^2} + (b-z)\frac{dw}{dz} - aw = 0</math>
<math>a=0</math>

<title>Hyperfocal distance</title>

           &amp; \dfrac{x-f}{c/2} &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{f}{D/2}  \\

\therefore &amp; x                &amp; = &amp; f+\dfrac{cf}{D}
\end{array}</math>
<math>\begin{array}{crclcl}
           &amp; \dfrac{H}{D/2} &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{x}{c/2}                                              \\
\therefore &amp; H              &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{Dx}{c}   &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{D}{c}\Big(f+\dfrac{cf}{D}\Big) \\
           &amp;                &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{Df}{c}+f &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{f^2}{Nc}+f
\end{array}</math>
<math>\begin{array}{crclcl}
           &amp; \dfrac{H}{D/2} &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{f}{c/2}                      \\
\therefore &amp; H              &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{Df}{c} &amp; = &amp; \dfrac{f^2}{Nc}
\end{array}</math>

<title>Steinhart–Hart equation</title>
<math>\frac{1}{T} = A + B \ln R + C (\ln R)^3,</math>
<math>R = \exp\left(\sqrt[3]{y - x} - \sqrt[3]{y + x}\right),</math>
<math>\begin{align}
  x &amp;= \frac{1}{2 C}\left(A - \frac{1}{T}\right), \\
  y &amp;= \sqrt{\left(\frac{B}{3C}\right)^3 + x^2}.
\end{align}</math>
<math>\begin{bmatrix}
    1 &amp; \ln R_1 &amp; \ln^3 R_1 \\
    1 &amp; \ln R_2 &amp; \ln^3 R_2 \\
    1 &amp; \ln R_3 &amp; \ln^3 R_3
 \end{bmatrix}\begin{bmatrix}
    A \\
    B \\
    C
 \end{bmatrix} = \begin{bmatrix}
   \frac{1}{T_1} \\
   \frac{1}{T_2} \\
   \frac{1}{T_3}
 \end{bmatrix}
</math>
<math>\begin{align}
            L_1 &amp;= \ln R_1, \quad L_2 = \ln R_2, \quad L_3 = \ln R_3 \\
            Y_1 &amp;= \frac{1}{T_1}, \quad Y_2 = \frac{1}{T_2}, \quad Y_3 = \frac{1}{T_3} \\
       \gamma_2 &amp;= \frac{Y_2 - Y_1}{L_2 - L_1}, \quad \gamma_3 = \frac{Y_3 - Y_1}{L_3 - L_1} \\
  \Rightarrow C &amp;= \left( \frac{ \gamma_3 - \gamma_2 }{ L_3 - L_2} \right) \left(L_1 + L_2 + L_3\right)^{-1} \\
  \Rightarrow B &amp;= \gamma_2 - C \left(L_1^2 + L_1 L_2 + L_2^2\right) \\
  \Rightarrow A &amp;= Y_1 - \left(B + L_1^2 C\right) L_1
\end{align}</math>

<math>\mathbf{J}_\mathrm{diffusion}(\mathbf{x})=-D(\mathbf{x}) \nabla \rho(\mathbf{x}),</math>
<math>\mathbf{J}_\mathrm{drift} + \mathbf{J}_\mathrm{diffusion} = 0</math>

<math>0 = \mathbf{J}_\mathrm{drift} + \mathbf{J}_\mathrm{diffusion} = -\mu \rho \nabla U - D \nabla \rho = \left(-\mu \rho - D \frac{\mathrm{d}\rho}{\mathrm{d} U}\right)\nabla U.</math>
<math>D = -\mu \frac{\rho}{\frac{\mathrm{d}\rho}{\mathrm{d} U}}.</math>

<math>\frac{\mathrm{d}\rho}{\mathrm{d} U} = -\frac{1}{k_{\rm B} T}\rho.</math>

<title>Enumerative combinatorics</title>
<math>F(x) = \sum^{\infty}_{n=0}f_nx^n</math>
<math>F(x) = \sum^{\infty}_{n=0}f_n\frac{x^n}{n!}</math>
<math>\mbox{Seq}(\mathcal{F}) = \epsilon\ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F} \ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F}\  \cup \cdots</math>
<math>1+F(x) + [F(x)]^2 + [F(x)]^3 + \cdots = \frac{1}{1-F(x)}</math>
<math>\mathcal{P} = \{\bullet\} \times \mbox{Seq}(\mathcal{P})</math>
<math>P(x) = x\frac{1}{1-P(x)}</math>
<math>P(x) = \frac{1-\sqrt{1-4x}}{2}</math>
<math>
\begin{align}
p_n &amp; = [x^n] P(x) = [x^n] \frac{1-\sqrt{1-4x}}{2} \\[6pt]
&amp; = [x^n] \frac{1}{2} - [x^n] \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{1-4x} \\[6pt]
&amp; = -\frac{1}{2} [x^n] \sum^{\infty}_{k=0} {\frac{1}{2} \choose k} (-4x)^k \\[6pt]
&amp; = -\frac{1}{2} {\frac{1}{2} \choose n} (-4)^n \\[6pt]
&amp; = \frac{1}{n} {2n-2 \choose n-1}
\end{align}
</math>

<title>Jordan's lemma</title>
<math>C_R = \{R e^{i \theta} \mid \theta \in [0, \pi]\}</math>
<math>f(z) = e^{i a z} g(z) , \quad z \in C_R ,</math>
<math>\left| \int_{C_R} f(z) \, dz \right| \le \frac{\pi}{a} M_R \quad \text{where} \quad M_R := \max_{\theta \in [0,\pi]} \left| g \left(R e^{i \theta}\right) \right| .</math>
<math>\lim_{R \to \infty} M_R = 0</math>
<math>\lim_{R \to \infty} \int_{C_R} f(z)\, dz = 0.</math>
<math>\oint_C f(z) \, dz = \int_{C_1}f(z)\,dz + \int_{C_2} f(z)\,dz\,.</math>
<math>\int_{C_2} f(z) \, dz = \int_{-R}^{R} f(x)\,dx\,.</math>
<math>\oint_{C} f(z)\, dz = 2\pi i \sum_{k=1}^n \operatorname{Res}(f, z_k)\,,</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^{\infty} f(x)\,dx = 2\pi i \sum_{k=1}^n \operatorname{Res}(f, z_k)\,.</math>
<math>f(z)=\frac{e^{iz}}{1+z^2},\qquad z\in{\mathbb C}\setminus\{i,-i\},</math>
<math>M_R=\max_{\theta\in[0,\pi]}\frac1{|1+R^2e^{2i\theta}|}=\frac1{R^2-1}\,,</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{e^{ix}}{1+x^2}\,dx=2\pi i\,\operatorname{Res}(f,i)\,.</math>
<math>\operatorname{Res}(f,i)=\lim_{z\to i}(z-i)f(z)
=\lim_{z\to i}\frac{e^{iz}}{z+i}=\frac{e^{-1}}{2i}</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{\cos x}{1+x^2}\,dx=\operatorname{Re}\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{e^{ix}}{1+x^2}\,dx=\frac{\pi}{e}\,.</math>
<math> \int_{C_R} f(z)\, dz
=\int_0^\pi g(Re^{i\theta})\,e^{iaR(\cos\theta+i \sin\theta)}\,i Re^{i\theta}\,d\theta
=R\int_0^\pi g(Re^{i\theta})\,e^{aR(i\cos\theta-\sin\theta)}\,ie^{i\theta}\,d\theta\,.
</math>
<math> I_R:=\biggl|\int_{C_R} f(z)\, dz\biggr|
\le R\int_0^\pi\bigl|g(Re^{i\theta})\,e^{aR(i\cos\theta-\sin\theta)}\,ie^{i\theta} \bigr|\,d\theta
=R\int_0^\pi \bigl|g(Re^{i\theta})\bigr|\,e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta\,.
</math>
<math> I_R \le RM_R\int_0^\pi e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta = 2RM_R\int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta\,.</math>
<math>I_R
\le 2RM_R \int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-2aR\theta/\pi}\,d\theta
=\frac{\pi}{a} (1-e^{-a R}) M_R\le\frac\pi{a}M_R\,.</math>

<title>Hubble–Reynolds law</title>
<math>I(R) = \frac{I_0}{(1+R/R_H)^2}</math>

<title>Galvanostat</title>
<math>{R} = {U \over I}</math>

<math> I = \frac{U}{R_x + R_{load}} </math>

<title>Linear–quadratic regulator</title>
<math>\dot{x} = Ax + Bu</math>
<math>J =  x^T(t_1)F(t_1)x(t_1)  + \int\limits_{t_0}^{t_1} \left( x^T Q x + u^T R u + 2 x^T N u \right) dt</math>
<math>u = -K x \,</math>
<math>K = R^{-1} (B^T P(t) + N^T) \,</math>
<math>A^T P(t) + P(t) A - (P(t) B + N) R^{-1} (B^T P(t) + N^T) + Q = - \dot{P}(t) \,</math>
<math>P(t_1) = F(t_1).</math>
<math>\dot{x} = Ax + Bu</math>
<math>-\dot{\lambda} = Qx + Nu + A^T \lambda </math>
<math> 0 = Ru + N^Tx + B^T \lambda</math>
<math> x(t_0) = x_0</math>
<math> \lambda(t_1) = F(t_1) x(t_1)</math>
<math>\dot{x} = Ax + Bu</math>
<math>J = \int_{0}^\infty \left( x^T Q x + u^T R u + 2 x^T N u \right) dt</math>
<math>u = -K x \,</math>
<math>K = R^{-1} (B^T P + N^T) \,</math>
<math>A^T P + P A - (P B + N) R^{-1} (B^T P + N^T) + Q = 0 \,</math>
<math>\mathcal A^T P + P \mathcal A - P B R^{-1} B^T P + \mathcal Q = 0 \,</math>
<math>\mathcal A = A - B R^{-1} N^T \qquad  \mathcal Q = Q - N R^{-1} N^T \,</math>
<math>x_{k+1} = A x_k + B u_k \,</math>
<math>J = x_N^T Q x_N + \sum\limits_{k=0}^{N-1} \left( x_k^T Q x_k + u_k^T R u_k + 2 x_k^T N u_k \right)</math>
<math>u_k = -F_k x_{k} \,</math>
<math>F_k = (R + B^T P_{k+1} B)^{-1} (B^T P_{k+1} A + N^T) \,</math>
<math>P_{k-1} = A^T P_k A - (A^T P_k B + N) \left( R + B^T P_k B \right)^{-1} (B^T P_k A + N^T) + Q </math>
<math>P_N = Q</math>
<math>x_{k+1} = A x_k + B u_k \,</math>
<math>J = \sum\limits_{k=0}^{\infty} \left( x_k^T Q x_k + u_k^T R u_k + 2 x_k^T N u_k \right)</math>
<math>u_k = -F x_k \,</math>
<math>F = (R + B^T P B)^{-1} (B^T P A + N^T) \,</math>
<math>P = A^T P A - (A^T P B + N) \left( R + B^T P B \right)^{-1} (B^T P A + N^T) + Q </math>
<math>P = \mathcal A^T P \mathcal A - \mathcal A^T P B \left( R + B^T P B \right)^{-1} B^T P \mathcal A + \mathcal Q </math>
<math> \mathcal A = A - B R^{-1} N^T \qquad \mathcal Q = Q - N R^{-1} N^T </math>

<math>\chi_\lambda=\chi_\mu</math>

<title>Collocation method</title>
<math> y'(t) = f(t,y(t)), \quad y(t_0)=y_0, </math>
<math>p(t_0) = y_0</math>
<math>p'(t_k) = f(t_k,p(t_k)) </math>
<math>t_k = t_0 + c_k h</math>
<math>k = 1, \ldots, n</math>
<math> p(t_0) = y_0, \, </math>
<math> p'(t_0) = f(t_0, p(t_0)), \, </math>
<math> p'(t_0+h) = f(t_0+h, p(t_0+h)). \, </math>
<math> p(t) = \alpha (t-t_0)^2 + \beta (t-t_0) + \gamma \, </math>
<math> 
   \begin{align}
   \alpha &amp;= \frac{1}{2h} \Big( f(t_0+h, p(t_0+h)) - f(t_0, p(t_0)) \Big), \\
   \beta &amp;= f(t_0, p(t_0)), \\
   \gamma &amp;= y_0. 
   \end{align} 
</math>
<math> y_1 = p(t_0 + h) = y_0 + \frac12h \Big (f(t_0+h, y_1) + f(t_0,y_0) \Big), \, </math>
<math> y(t) = y(t_0) + \int_{t_0}^t f(\tau, y(\tau)) \,\textrm{d}\tau, \, </math>

<title>Hydrostatic stress</title>
<math>\sigma_h = \displaystyle\sum_{i=1}^n \rho_i g h_i</math>
<math>\sigma_h = \rho_w g h_w =1000 \,\text{kg m}^{-3} \cdot 9.8 \,\text{m s}^{-2} \cdot 10 \,\text{m} =9.8 \cdot {10^4} \text{ kg m}^{-1} \text{s}^{-2} =9.8 \cdot 10^4 \text{ N m}^{-2} </math>
<math>\sigma_h \cdot I_3 =
\sigma_h \left[ \begin{array}{ccc}
1 &amp; 0 &amp; 0 \\
0 &amp; 1 &amp; 0 \\
0 &amp; 0 &amp; 1 \end{array} \right] = 
\left[ \begin{array}{ccc}
\sigma_h &amp; 0 &amp; 0 \\
0 &amp; \sigma_h &amp; 0 \\
0 &amp; 0 &amp; \sigma_h \end{array} \right]
</math>

<title>Riesz mean</title>
<math>s^\delta(\lambda) = 
\sum_{n\le \lambda} \left(1-\frac{n}{\lambda}\right)^\delta s_n </math>
<math>R_n = \frac{1}{\lambda_n} \sum_{k=0}^n (\lambda_k-\lambda_{k-1})^\delta s_k</math>
<math>s_n = \sum_{k=0}^n a_k</math>
<math>a_n=1</math>
<math> 
\sum_{n\le \lambda} \left(1-\frac{n}{\lambda}\right)^\delta
= \frac{1}{2\pi i} \int_{c-i\infty}^{c+i\infty} 
\frac{\Gamma(1+\delta)\Gamma(s)}{\Gamma(1+\delta+s)} \zeta(s) \lambda^s \, ds
= \frac{\lambda}{1+\delta} + \sum_n b_n \lambda^{-n}.
</math>
<math>a_n=\Lambda(n)</math>
<math> 
\sum_{n\le \lambda} \left(1-\frac{n}{\lambda}\right)^\delta \Lambda(n)
= - \frac{1}{2\pi i} \int_{c-i\infty}^{c+i\infty} 
\frac{\Gamma(1+\delta)\Gamma(s)}{\Gamma(1+\delta+s)} 
\frac{\zeta^\prime(s)}{\zeta(s)} \lambda^s \, ds
= \frac{\lambda}{1+\delta} + 
\sum_\rho \frac {\Gamma(1+\delta)\Gamma(\rho)}{\Gamma(1+\delta+\rho)}
+\sum_n c_n \lambda^{-n}.
</math>

<title>Poisson–Boltzmann equation</title>
<math>\nabla^2\psi = \frac{\partial^2\psi}{\partial x^2} + \frac{\partial^2\psi}{\partial y^2} + \frac{\partial^2\psi}{\partial z^2}  = -\frac{\rho_e}{\epsilon_r\epsilon_0}, </math>
<math>c_i = c^0_i \cdot e^\frac{-W_i}{k_BT},</math>
<math> W^+ = e\psi </math>
<math> W^- = -e\psi </math>
<math> c^- = c_0 \cdot e^\frac{e\psi(x,y,z)}{k_BT}</math>
<math> c^+ = c_0 \cdot e^\frac{-e\psi(x,y,z)}{k_BT}</math>
<math> \rho_e = e{(c^+ - c^-)} = c_0e \cdot \left[e^\frac{-e\psi(x,y,z)}{k_BT} - e^\frac{e\psi(x,y,z)}{k_BT}\right]. </math>
<math>\frac{d^2\psi}{dr^2} + \frac{L}{r}\frac{d\psi}{dr} = e^\psi-\delta e^{-\psi}</math>
<math>\psi=\frac{e\Phi}{kT}</math>
<math>R_{eD}=\sqrt{\frac{kT}{4\pi e^2 n_{e0}}}</math>
<math>\psi=\psi_0e^{-\Kappa x}</math>
<math>\Kappa=\sqrt{\frac{2c_0e^2}{\epsilon\epsilon_0k_BT}}</math>
<math>\lambda_D=\Kappa^{-1}</math>
<math>\lambda_D=\frac{0.304nm}{\sqrt{c_0\frac{L}{mol}}}</math>
<math>\Kappa=\sqrt{\frac{e^2}{\epsilon\epsilon_0k_BT}\Sigma c_i{Z_i}^2}</math>
<math>y\equiv\frac{e\psi}{k_BT}</math>
<math>e^{-\Kappa x}=\frac{(e^{y/2}-1) (e^{y_0/2}+1)}{(e^{y/2}+1 )(e^{y_0/2}-1)}</math>
<math>e^{y/2}=\frac{e^{y_0/2}+1+(e^{y_0/2}-1)*e^{-\Kappa x}}{e^{y_0/2}+1-(e^{y_0/2}-1)*e^{-\Kappa x}}</math>
<math>y=2\ln \frac{e^{y_0/2}+1+(e^{y_0/2}-1)*e^{-\Kappa x}}{e^{y_0/2}+1-(e^{y_0/2}-1)*e^{-\Kappa x}}</math>
<math>y\equiv\frac{e\psi}{k_BT}</math>
<math>\psi=\frac{2k_BT}{e}*\ln \frac{e^{y_0/2}+1+(e^{y_0/2}-1)*e^{-\Kappa x}}{e^{y_0/2}+1-(e^{y_0/2}-1)*e^{-\Kappa x}}</math>
<math>y_0=\frac{e\psi_0}{k_BT}</math>
<math>\Delta G^{el} = \int\limits^\tau qU (\tau^\prime)\,d\tau^\prime</math>
<math>\Delta G^{el} = \int\limits_V (kT\sum_i c_i^\infty[1 - \exp(\frac{-z_i qU}{kT})] + p^f U - \frac{-\epsilon(\vec{\nabla} U)^2}{8 \pi})dV</math>
<math>\Delta G^{el} = \Delta G^{ef} + \Delta G^{em} + \Delta G^{mob} + \Delta G^{solv}</math>
<math>\Delta G^{ef} = \int\limits_V \frac{p^f U}{2} dV</math>
<math>\Delta G^{em} = \int\limits_V \frac{\sum_i c_i z_i qU}{2} dV</math>
<math>\Delta G^{mob} = kT\int\limits_V c_i \ln\frac{c_i}{c_i^{\infty}} dV</math>
<math>\Delta G^{solv} = kT\int\limits_V \sum_i c_i^{\infty}[1 - \exp(\frac{-z_i qU}{kT})]dV</math>
<math>\Delta G^{out} = \Delta G^{em} + \Delta G^{mob} + \Delta G^{solv}</math>

<title>Coble creep</title>
<math>\frac{d\epsilon_C}{dt} \equiv \dot{\epsilon_C} = A_C\frac{\delta'}{d^3}\frac{\sigma\Omega}{kT}D_0e^{-(Q_f+Q_m)/kT} = A_C\frac{\delta'}{d^3}\frac{\sigma\Omega}{kT}D_{GB},</math>
<math>\frac{d\epsilon_C}{dt} \equiv \dot{\epsilon_C} = A_C\frac{\delta'}{d^3}\frac{\sigma\Omega}{kT}D_0e^{-(Q_f+Q_m)/kT} = A_C\frac{\delta'}{d^3}\frac{\sigma\Omega}{kT}D_{GB},</math>
<math>D_{GB} = D_0e^{-(Q_f+Q_m)/kT}</math>
<math>\Delta C = C_0 \frac{\sigma\Omega}{kT}</math>
<math>
J_v = A' D_v \frac{\Delta C}{\pi R/2}\delta' (2\pi R)
</math>
<math>
J_v\Omega = \pi R^2 dR/dt = \pi R^3 \dot{\epsilon}
</math>
<math>\dot{\epsilon} = (1/R)(dR/dt)</math>
<math> 
\dot{\epsilon}_C = \frac{J_v\Omega}{\pi R^3} = A D_v\Delta C\Omega\frac{\delta'}{R^3} = A D_{GB}\frac{\sigma\Omega}{kT}\frac{\delta'}{R^3}
</math>
<math>D_{GB}=D_v C_0\Omega</math>
<math>
\dot{\epsilon_{GS}} \propto \frac{\Omega}{kT}\frac{\delta'D_{GB}}{d^3}(\sigma-\frac{0.72\gamma}{d})
</math>

<title>Pauli equation</title>
<math>\left[ \frac{1}{2m}(\boldsymbol{\sigma}\cdot(\mathbf{p} - q \mathbf{A}))^2 + q \phi \right] |\psi\rangle = i \hbar \frac{\partial}{\partial t} |\psi\rangle  </math>
<math>\boldsymbol{\sigma} = (\sigma_x, \sigma_y, \sigma_z)</math>
<math>\mathbf{p} = -i\hbar \nabla</math>
<math> |\psi\rangle = \begin{bmatrix} 
\psi_+ \\
\psi_-
\end{bmatrix}</math>
<math>\hat{H} = \frac{1}{2m} \left[\boldsymbol{\sigma}\cdot(\mathbf{p} - q \mathbf{A}) \right]^2 + q \phi</math>
<math>\mathbf{P} = p - q\mathbf{A}</math>
<math>(\boldsymbol{\sigma}\cdot \mathbf{a})(\boldsymbol{\sigma}\cdot \mathbf{b}) =  \mathbf{a}\cdot\mathbf{b} + i\boldsymbol{\sigma}\cdot \left(\mathbf{a} \times \mathbf{b}\right)</math>
<math>\hat{H} |\psi\rangle = \left[\frac{1}{2m}\left[\left(\mathbf{p} - q \mathbf{A}\right)^2 - q \hbar \boldsymbol{\sigma}\cdot \mathbf{B}\right] + q \phi\right]|\psi\rangle = i \hbar \frac{\partial}{\partial t} |\psi\rangle</math>
<math>\mathbf{B} = \nabla \times \mathbf{A}</math>
<math>\left( \frac{\mathbf{p}^2}{2m} + q \phi \right) \begin{bmatrix} 
\psi_+ \\
\psi_-
\end{bmatrix} = i \hbar \frac{\partial}{\partial t} \begin{bmatrix} 
\psi_+ \\
\psi_-
\end{bmatrix}.</math>
<math>
\underbrace{i \hbar \frac{\partial}{\partial t} |\psi_\pm\rangle = \left( \frac{( \mathbf{p} -q \mathbf A)^2}{2 m} + q \phi \right) \mathbb{I} \mathbf |\psi\rangle }_\mathrm{Schr\ddot{o}dinger~equation} - \underbrace{\frac{q \hbar}{2m}\boldsymbol{\sigma} \cdot \mathbf B \mathbf |\psi\rangle }_\mathrm{Stern-Gerlach \, term}</math>
<math> \mathbb{I} = \begin{pmatrix}
1 &amp; 0 \\
0 &amp; 1 \\
\end{pmatrix} </math>

<title>Impedance parameters</title>
<math>V = Z I\,</math>
<math>{V_1 \choose V_2} = \begin{pmatrix} Z_{11} &amp; Z_{12} \\ Z_{21} &amp; Z_{22} \end{pmatrix}{I_1 \choose I_2} </math>
<math>Z_{11} = {V_1 \over I_1 } \bigg|_{I_2 = 0} \qquad Z_{12} = {V_1 \over I_2 } \bigg|_{I_1 = 0}</math>
<math>Z_{21} = {V_2 \over I_1 } \bigg|_{I_2 = 0} \qquad Z_{22} = {V_2 \over I_2 } \bigg|_{I_1 = 0}</math>
<math>Z_{nm} = {V_n \over I_m } \bigg|_{I_k = 0 \text{ for } k \ne m}</math>
<math>Z_\text{in} = Z_{11} - \frac{Z_{12}Z_{21}}{Z_{22}+Z_L}</math>
<math>Z_\text{out} = Z_{22} - \frac{Z_{12}Z_{21}}{Z_{11}+Z_S}</math>
<math> \begin{align}
Z &amp;= \sqrt{z} (1_{\!N} + S) (1_{\!N} - S)^{-1} \sqrt{z} \\
  &amp;= \sqrt{z} (1_{\!N} - S)^{-1} (1_{\!N} + S) \sqrt{z} \\
\end{align} </math>
<math> \begin{align}
S &amp;= (\sqrt{y}Z\sqrt{y} \,- 1_{\!N}) (\sqrt{y}Z\sqrt{y} \,+ 1_{\!N})^{-1} \\
  &amp;= (\sqrt{y}Z\sqrt{y} \,+ 1_{\!N})^{-1} (\sqrt{y}Z\sqrt{y} \,- 1_{\!N}) \\
\end{align} </math>
<math>\sqrt{z} = \begin{pmatrix}
 \sqrt{z_{01}} &amp;  \\
               &amp; \sqrt{z_{02}} \\
               &amp;            &amp; \ddots \\
               &amp;            &amp;           &amp; \sqrt{z_{0N}}
\end{pmatrix}
</math>
<math>\sqrt{y} = (\sqrt{z})^{-1}</math>
<math>z_{01} = z_{02} = Z_0</math>
<math>Z_{11} = {((1 + S_{11}) (1 - S_{22}) + S_{12} S_{21}) \over \Delta_S} Z_0 \,</math>
<math>Z_{12} = {2 S_{12} \over \Delta_S} Z_0 \,</math>
<math>Z_{21} = {2 S_{21} \over \Delta_S} Z_0 \,</math>
<math>Z_{22} = {((1 - S_{11}) (1 + S_{22}) + S_{12} S_{21}) \over \Delta_S} Z_0 \,</math>
<math>\Delta_S = (1 - S_{11}) (1 - S_{22}) - S_{12} S_{21} \,</math>
<math>S_{11} = {(Z_{11} - Z_0) (Z_{22} + Z_0) - Z_{12} Z_{21} \over \Delta}</math>
<math>S_{12} = {2 Z_0 Z_{12} \over \Delta} \,</math>
<math>S_{21} = {2 Z_0 Z_{21} \over \Delta} \,</math>
<math>S_{22} = {(Z_{11} + Z_0) (Z_{22} - Z_0) - Z_{12} Z_{21} \over \Delta}</math>
<math>\Delta = (Z_{11} + Z_0) (Z_{22} + Z_0) - Z_{12} Z_{21} \, </math>
<math>Z_{11} = {Y_{22} \over \Delta_Y} \,</math>
<math>Z_{12} = {-Y_{12} \over \Delta_Y} \,</math>
<math>Z_{21} = {-Y_{21} \over \Delta_Y} \,</math>
<math>Z_{22} = {Y_{11} \over \Delta_Y} \,</math>
<math>\Delta_Y = Y_{11} Y_{22} - Y_{12} Y_{21} \,</math>

<title>Magnetic anisotropy</title>

<title>Lemaître coordinates</title>
<math>ds^2=\left(1-{r_s\over r}\right)dt^2-{dr^2\over 1-{r_s\over r}} - r^2\left(d\theta^2+\sin^2\theta d\phi^2\right) \;,</math>

<math>s_q(x) = \begin{cases} 0 &amp; \text{if }  x &lt; -\nu  \\ \frac{1}{c(q)}E_{q^2}^{\frac{-q^2x^2}{[2]_q}}  &amp; \text{if } -\nu \leq x \leq \nu \\ 0 &amp; \mbox{if } x &gt;\nu. \end{cases} </math>

1 &amp; \text{if } x&gt;\nu
\end{cases}</math>
<math>G_q(x)= \begin{cases}  0 &amp; \text{if } x &lt; -\nu, \\

1 &amp; \text{if}\ x &gt; \nu
\end{cases}</math>

<title>Combinatoria enumerativa</title>
<math>F(x) = \sum^{\infty}_{n=0}f_nx^n</math>
<math>F(x) = \sum^{\infty}_{n=0}f_n\frac{x^n}{n!}</math>
<math>\mbox{Seq}(\mathcal{F}) = \epsilon\ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F} \ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F}\  \cup \cdots</math>
<math>1+F(x) + [F(x)]^2 + [F(x)]^3 + \cdots = \frac{1}{1-F(x)}</math>
<math>\mathcal{P} = \{\bullet\} \times \mbox{Seq}(\mathcal{P})</math>
<math>P(x) = x\frac{1}{1-P(x)}</math>
<math>P(x) = \frac{1-\sqrt{1-4x}}{2}</math>
<math>\begin{align}
p_n &amp; = [x^n] P(x) = [x^n] \frac{1-\sqrt{1-4x}}{2} \\[6pt]
&amp; = [x^n] \frac{1}{2} - [x^n] \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{1-4x} \\[6pt]
&amp; = -\frac{1}{2} [x^n] \sum^{\infty}_{k=0} {\frac{1}{2} \choose k} (-4x)^k \\[6pt]
&amp; = -\frac{1}{2} {\frac{1}{2} \choose n} (-4)^n \\[6pt]
&amp; = \frac{1}{n} {2n-2 \choose n-1}
\end{align}</math>

<title>Lemme de Jordan</title>
<math>\lim_{r \to \infty}\oint_{C(0,r)\cap D }f(z)dz = 0</math>
<math>\oint_{C(0,r)\cap D }f(z)dz=\oint_{C(0,r)\cap D }zf(z)\frac{dz}{z}.</math>
<math>z=r e^{i\theta}</math>
<math>\left|\oint_{C(0,r)\cap D }zf(z)\frac{dz}{z}\right| \leqslant \int_0^{2\pi}|zf(z)|\frac{rd\theta}{r}= 2\pi \max_{z \in C(0,r)}|zf(z)| \to 0</math>
<math>\left|\oint_{C(0,r)\cap D }zf(z)\frac{dz}{z}\right| \leqslant \int_0^{2\pi}|zf(z)|\frac{rd\theta}{r}= 2\pi \max_{z \in C(0,r)}|zf(z)| \to 0</math>
<math>f(z)=e^{iaz}g(z)</math>
<math>\lim_{r \to \infty} \oint_{C(0,r) \cap D} f(z)\, dz = 0</math>
<math>z=re^{i\theta}</math>
<math>\left|\int_{C(0,r)\cap D} f(z)\, dz\right| \leqslant  \int_{C(0,r)\cap D} |f(z)|\, dz \leqslant \int_{\theta_1(r)}^{\theta_2(r)} |g(re^{i\theta})|e^{ar(i\cos\theta-\sin\theta)}re^{i\theta}|\,d\theta</math>
<math>\left|\int_{C(0,r)} f(z)\, dz\right|\leqslant \int_0^\pi \left|g(re^{i\theta})\right|e^{-ar\sin\theta}\ r\,d\theta</math>
<math>M(r) = \max_{\theta\in[0,\pi]}\left|g(re^{i\theta})\right|</math>
<math>\left|\int_{C(0,r)} f(z)\, dz\right| \leqslant M(r) \int_0^\pi e^{-ar\sin\theta}\ r\,d\theta = 2 M(r) \int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-ar\sin\theta}\ r\,d\theta</math>
<math>\left|\int_{C(0,r)} f(z)\, dz\right| \leqslant M(r) \int_0^\pi e^{-ar\sin\theta}\ r\,d\theta = 2 M(r) \int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-ar\sin\theta}\ r\,d\theta</math>
<math>\sin\theta\geqslant \frac{2\theta}{\pi}, \quad  0\leqslant\theta\leqslant\frac{\pi}{2}</math>
<math>\sin\theta\geqslant \frac{2\theta}{\pi}, \quad  0\leqslant\theta\leqslant\frac{\pi}{2}</math>
<math>\left|\int_{C(0,r)} f(z)\, dz\right| \leqslant 2 M(r) \int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-2ar\theta/\pi}\ r\,d\theta = \frac{\pi}{a} (1-e^{-a r}) M(r)</math>
<math>\left|\int_{C(0,r)} f(z)\, dz\right| \leqslant 2 M(r) \int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-2ar\theta/\pi}\ r\,d\theta = \frac{\pi}{a} (1-e^{-a r}) M(r)</math>
<math>\lim_{r \to\infty} \left|\int_{C(0,r)} f(z)\, dz\right| \leqslant \frac{\pi}{a} \lim_{r \to\infty} M(r) = 0</math>
<math>\lim_{r \to\infty} \left|\int_{C(0,r)} f(z)\, dz\right| \leqslant \frac{\pi}{a} \lim_{r \to\infty} M(r) = 0</math>

<math>\left|\oint_{C(a,r)}f(z)(z-a)\frac{dz}{z-a}\right| \leqslant \int_0^{2\pi}|f(z)(z-a)|\frac{rd\theta}{r}= 2\pi \max_{z \in C(0,r)}|f(z)(z-a)| \to 0</math>
<math>\int_C f(z)dz = \int_C zf(z) \frac{dz}{z} &lt; M \frac{2\pi R}{R} &lt; 2\pi M</math>

<title>Équation de Pauli</title>
<math>\Psi(t,\vec{r}) = \binom{\Psi_+}{\Psi_-}</math>
<math>\mathbb A = \left( U(\vec r,t) , \vec A(\vec r,t)\right)</math>
<math>\vec B = \nabla \times  \vec A</math>
<math>\vec \sigma = \left( \sigma_1 , \sigma_2 , \sigma_3 \right)</math>
<math>
i\hbar{\partial\Psi(\vec{r},t)\over\partial t}= \left( {1\over 2m}\left( \vec P + q\vec A(\vec{r},t) \right)^2 + qU(\vec r,t) - {q\hbar\over2m} \vec \sigma . \vec B(\vec r,t) \right)\Psi(\vec{r},t)
</math>
<math>
H= {1\over 2m}\left(\vec \sigma .[\vec P -q\vec A(\vec r,t)] \right)^2 + qU(\vec r,t)
</math>
<math>\vec\sigma.\vec B=\vec\sigma.(\vec\nabla\times\vec A)=\sigma_x[\vec\nabla \times \vec A]_x+\sigma_y[\vec\nabla \times \vec A]_y+\sigma_z[\vec\nabla \times \vec A]_z</math>
<math>\sigma_x=  \begin{pmatrix} 0 &amp; 1 \\ 1 &amp; 0 \end{pmatrix}         \quad\sigma_y=\begin{pmatrix} 0 &amp; -i \\ i &amp; 0 \end{pmatrix}\quad\sigma_z=\begin{pmatrix} 1 &amp; 0 \\ 0 &amp; -1 \end{pmatrix} </math>
<math>\vec\nabla \times \vec A=\begin{pmatrix} \nabla_y A_z-\nabla_z A_y \\ \nabla_z A_x-\nabla_x A_z\\ \nabla_x A_y-\nabla_y A_x \end{pmatrix}</math>
<math>\Rightarrow \vec\sigma.\vec B=\begin{pmatrix} (\vec\nabla \times \vec A)_z &amp; (\vec\nabla \times \vec A)_x-i(\vec\nabla \times \vec A)_y \\ (\vec\nabla \times \vec A)_x+i(\vec\nabla \times \vec A)_y &amp; -(\vec\nabla \times \vec A)_z\end{pmatrix}</math>
<math>=\begin{pmatrix} \nabla_x A_y -\nabla_y A_x &amp; \nabla_y A_z -\nabla_z A_y -i(\nabla_z A_x-\nabla_x A_z) \\ \nabla_y A_z -\nabla_z A_y +i(\nabla_z A_x-\nabla_x A_z) &amp; -\nabla_x A_y +\nabla_y A_x\end{pmatrix}</math>
<math> [\psi](\vec r)=\begin{pmatrix} \psi_+(\vec r)\\ \psi_-(\vec r) \end{pmatrix}</math>
<math>(\nabla_x A_y-\nabla_y A_x)\psi_+=\nabla_x A_y\psi_+-\nabla_y A_x\psi_+</math>
<math>=\nabla_x(A_y\psi_+)-A_y \nabla_x\psi_+ -\nabla_y(A_x\psi_+) +A_x\nabla_y \psi_+</math>
<math>= [\nabla_x A_y -\nabla_y A_x+A_x\nabla_y-A_y \nabla_x]\psi_+=[[\vec\nabla \times \vec A]_z+[\vec A\times\vec\nabla ]_z]\psi_+</math>
<math>\nabla_y A_z\psi_- -\nabla_z A_y\psi_- -i(\nabla_z A_x\psi_--\nabla_x A_z\psi_-)=
:\nabla_y( A_z\psi_-)-A_z\nabla_y\psi_- -\nabla_z( A_y\psi_-)</math>
<math>=[(\vec\nabla \times \vec A)_x+(\vec A\times\vec\nabla)_x]\psi_--i[(\vec\nabla \times \vec A)_y+(\vec A\times\vec\nabla)_y]\psi_-</math>
<math>\vec\sigma.\vec B=\vec\sigma(\vec\nabla \times \vec A)+\vec\sigma(\vec A \times\vec\nabla ) </math>
<math>\vec P = \frac{\hbar}{i} \vec\nabla \Rightarrow </math>
<math>\vec\sigma.\vec B =\frac{i}{q\hbar}.\vec\sigma [(\vec P \times q\vec A)+(q\vec A \times \vec P)]=-\frac{i}{q\hbar}.\vec\sigma[(\vec P -q\vec A)\times (\vec P- q\vec A)]</math>
<math>(\vec\sigma.\vec M)(\vec\sigma.\vec N)=\vec M.\vec NI+i\vec\sigma(\vec M \times\vec N)</math>
<math> \Rightarrow i\vec\sigma [(\vec P -q\vec A)\times (\vec P- q\vec A)]=(\vec\sigma.(\vec P -q\vec A))^2-(\vec P -q\vec A)^2I</math>
<math> \Rightarrow \vec\sigma \vec B= -\frac {1}{q\hbar}[\vec\sigma (\vec P -q\vec A)]^2+\frac {1}{q\hbar}[\vec P -q\vec A]^2I </math>
<math>H=\frac {1}{2m}[\vec P -q\vec A]^2 +qU-\frac {q \hbar}{2m}\vec\sigma .\vec B</math>
<math>=\frac {1}{2m}[\vec P -q\vec A]^2 +qU+\frac {1}{2m}[\vec\sigma (\vec P -q\vec A)]^2-\frac {1}{2m}[\vec P -q\vec A]^2I </math>
<math>=\frac {1}{2m}[\vec\sigma (\vec P -q\vec A(\vec r,t))]^2+qU(\vec r,t)</math>

<title>Déterminant de Hurwitz</title>
<math>
P(\lambda)= a_n \lambda^n + a_{n-1} \lambda^{n-1} + \dots + a_1 \lambda + a_0
</math>
<math>
H=
\begin{pmatrix}
a_{n-1} &amp; a_{n-3} &amp; a_{n-5} &amp; \dots &amp; \dots &amp; 0 &amp; \dots &amp; 0 \\
a_n &amp; a_{n-2} &amp; a_{n-4} &amp; &amp; &amp; \vdots &amp; &amp; \vdots \\
0 &amp; a_{n-1} &amp; a_{n-3} &amp; &amp; &amp; 0 &amp; &amp; \vdots \\
\vdots &amp; a_n &amp; &amp; \ddots &amp; &amp; a_0 &amp; \vdots &amp; \vdots \\
\vdots &amp; 0 &amp; &amp; &amp; \ddots &amp; a_1 &amp; 0 &amp; \vdots \\
\vdots &amp; \vdots  &amp; 0 &amp; &amp; &amp; a_2 &amp; a_0 &amp; \vdots \\
\vdots &amp; \vdots &amp; \vdots &amp; &amp; &amp; a_3 &amp; a_1 &amp; 0 \\

\end{pmatrix}.

<title>Métrique de Lemaître</title>
<math>ds^2 = c^2.dT^2 - \frac{dR^2}{\left( \frac{3}{2R_S}(R-cT) \right)^{2/3}} - \left( \textstyle\frac{3}{2}. (R-cT) \right)^{4/3}.R_S^{2/3}.(d\theta^2 + sin^2 \theta .d\phi^2 )</math>
<math>ds^2 = c^2.dT^2 - \frac{dR^2}{B} - B^2 {R_S}^2 (d\theta^2 + sin^2 \theta .d\phi^2 )</math>
<math>B = \left( \frac{3}{2R_S}(R-cT) \right)^{2/3}</math>
<math>~c.dT = c.dt+\frac{f(r).dr}{1-\textstyle\frac{R_S}{r}}~</math>
<math>~dR = c.dt+\frac{dr}{f(r).(1-\textstyle\frac{R_S}{r})}~</math>
<math>ds^2 = \frac{1-\textstyle\frac{R_S}{r}}{1-f^2(r)}.\left(c^2.dT^2-f^2(r).dR^2 \right)-r^2.(d\theta^2 + sin^2 \theta .d\phi^2 )</math>
<math>f(r)= \sqrt{ \frac{R_S}{r}}</math>
<math>R-c.T={\textstyle\frac{2}{3}} . \frac{r^{3/2}}{R_S^{1/2}}</math>
<math>r= \left( {\textstyle\frac{3}{2}} .(R-c.T) \right)^{2/3}.R_s^{1/3} = B.R_S</math>
<math>t = \frac {R_S}{c} \left( -\frac{2}{3} B^{1/2} + \ln \left| \frac{B^{1/2}+1}{B^{1/2}-1}\right| + \frac {R}{R_S}\right)</math>
<math>B = \left( \frac{3}{2R_S}(R-cT) \right)^{2/3}</math>
<math>R-c.T= constante</math>
<math>r = constant</math>
<math>R-c.T= 0</math>
<math>r=0</math>
<math>r=R_S</math>
<math>R-c.T= {\textstyle\frac{2}{3}}.R_S</math>
<math>ds^2=0</math>
<math>\textstyle{\frac{dR}{c.dT} = \pm \sqrt{\frac{r}{R_S}}}</math>
<math>R-c.T= constante</math>
<math>\textstyle{\frac{dR}{c.dT} = 1 \in \left]-\sqrt{\frac{r}{R_S}} ; +\sqrt{\frac{r}{R_S}} \right[}</math>
<math>R-c.T= constante</math>
<math>r=0</math>
<math>r=R_S</math>
<math>~c.dT = -\left( c.dt+\frac{f(r).dr}{1-\textstyle\frac{R_S}{r}} \right)~</math>
<math>~dR = c.dt+\frac{dr}{f(r).(1-\textstyle\frac{R_S}{r})}~</math>
<math>~dR = c.dt+\frac{dr}{f(r).(1-\textstyle\frac{R_S}{r})} = 0~</math>
<math>0&lt; r \leqslant R_S</math>

<title>Fonction de Massieu</title>
<math>\mathrm{d} U = \delta W + \delta Q</math>
<math>\delta W = \delta W_P + \delta W_g + \delta W_{em} + \cdots</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U + \mathrm{d} U_\text{ext} = 0</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} S = {\delta Q \over T}</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} S \geq { \delta Q \over T}</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext} \geq 0</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext} = 0</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} V + \mathrm{d} V_\text{ext} = 0</math>
<math>\delta W = - P \, \mathrm{d} V</math>
<math>-\delta W = P \, \mathrm{d} V = - P \, \mathrm{d} V_\text{ext}</math>
<math> - \delta Q = T \, \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext}</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U_\text{ext} = - P \, \mathrm{d} V_\text{ext} + T \, \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext}</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U = \delta W + \delta Q</math>
<math>\delta W = - P \, \mathrm{d} V</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U = - P \, \mathrm{d} V + T \, \mathrm{d} S - \left[T \, \mathrm{d} S - \delta Q \right]</math>
<math>T \, \mathrm{d} S - \delta Q = T \left[ \mathrm{d} S - { \delta Q \over T } \right] = T \left[ \mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext} \right] \geq 0</math>
<math>T \, \mathrm{d} S - \delta Q = T \left[ \mathrm{d} S - { \delta Q \over T } \right] = T \left[ \mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext} \right] \geq 0</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U + P \, \mathrm{d} V - T \, \mathrm{d} S = - T \left[\mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext} \right] \leq 0 </math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U + P \, \mathrm{d} V - T \, \mathrm{d} S = - T \left[\mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext} \right] \leq 0 </math>
<math>\mathrm{d} \Psi = \mathrm{d} S - {\mathrm{d} U \over T} - {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V = \mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} S_\text{ext}</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} \Psi \geq 0</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} \Psi = \mathrm{d} S - {\mathrm{d} U \over T} - {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} V = 0</math>
<math>- {\mathrm{d} U \over T} = \mathrm{d} \! \left( - {U \over T} \right)</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} \Psi = \mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} \! \left( - {U \over T} \right) = \mathrm{d} \! \left[ S - {U \over T} \right]</math>
<math>J = S - {U \over T} = - {F \over T}</math>
<math>F = U-TS</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} J \geq 0</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} J = \mathrm{d} S - {\mathrm{d} U \over T} - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right)</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U = - P \, \mathrm{d} V + T \, \mathrm{d} S + \sum_{i=1}^{N} \mu_i \, \mathrm{d} n_i - \left[T \, \mathrm{d} S - \delta Q \right]</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} J = {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i + \left[\mathrm{d} S - {\delta Q \over T} \right]</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} J = {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} J &gt; {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i</math>
<math>J = J \! \left( V, {1 \over T}, n \right)</math>
<math>- {\mathrm{d} U \over T} = \mathrm{d} \! \left( - {U \over T} \right)</math>
<math>- {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V = \mathrm{d} \! \left( {- PV \over T} \right)</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} \Psi = \mathrm{d} S + \mathrm{d} \! \left( - {U \over T} \right) + \mathrm{d} \! \left( {- PV \over T} \right) = \mathrm{d} \! \left[ S - {U \over T} - {PV \over T} \right]</math>
<math>Y = S - {U \over T} - {PV \over T}= - {G \over T}</math>
<math>G = U+PV-TS</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y \geq 0</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y = \mathrm{d} S - {\mathrm{d} U \over T} - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right) - {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V - V \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T } \right)</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U = - P \, \mathrm{d} V + T \, \mathrm{d} S  + \sum_{i=1}^{N} \mu_i \, \mathrm{d} n_i - \left[T \, \mathrm{d} S - \delta Q \right]</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y = -V \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T } \right) - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i + \left[\mathrm{d} S - {\delta Q \over T} \right]</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y = -V \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T } \right) - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y &gt; -V \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T } \right) - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i</math>
<math>Y = Y \! \left( {P \over T}, {1 \over T}, n \right)</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T} \right) = {\mathrm{d} P \over T} + P \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right)</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y = -V \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T } \right) - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i + \left[\mathrm{d} S - {\delta Q \over T} \right]</math>
<math>= -{V \over T} \, \mathrm{d} \! P - \left[ U + PV \right] \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i + \left[\mathrm{d} S - {\delta Q \over T} \right]</math>
<math>= -{V \over T} \, \mathrm{d} \! P - H \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i + \left[\mathrm{d} S - {\delta Q \over T} \right]</math>
<math>H = U + PV</math>
<math>Y = Y \! \left( P, {1 \over T}, n \right)</math>
<math>y = f \! \left( x \right)</math>
<math>p = f^\prime \! \left( x \right)</math>
<math>x = f^\prime{}^{-1} \! \left( p \right)</math>
<math>g \! \left( p \right) = f \! \left( x \right) - p \cdot x</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} U = - P \, \mathrm{d} V + T \, \mathrm{d} S + \sum_{i=1}^{N} \mu_i \, \mathrm{d} n_i</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} S = {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V  + {1 \over T} \, \mathrm{d} U - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i</math>
<math>S = f \! \left( V, U, n \right)</math>
<math>\left( {\partial S \over \partial V} \right)_{U,n} = {P \over T}</math>
<math>\left( {\partial S \over \partial U} \right)_{V,n} = {1 \over T}</math>
<math>\left( {\partial S \over \partial n_i} \right)_{V,U,n_{j \neq j}} = -{\mu_i \over T}</math>
<math>g_1 \! \left( V, {1 \over T}, n \right) = S - \left( {\partial S \over \partial U} \right)_{V,n} \cdot U
= S -{1 \over T} U = J \! \left( V, {1 \over T}, n \right)</math>
<math>g_2 \! \left( V, {1 \over T}, n \right) = S - \left( {\partial S \over \partial V} \right)_{U,n} \cdot V - \left( {\partial S \over \partial U} \right)_{V,n} \cdot U
= S -{P \over T} V -{1 \over T} U = Y \! \left( {P \over T}, {1 \over T}, n \right)</math>
<math>g_3 \! \left( {P \over T}, U, n \right) = S - \left( {\partial S \over \partial V} \right)_{U,n} \cdot V
= S -{P \over T} V = \Psi_1 \! \left( {P \over T}, U, n \right)</math>
<math>g_4 \! \left( V, {1 \over T}, {\mu \over T} \right) = S - \left( {\partial S \over \partial U} \right)_{V,n} \cdot U
- \sum_{i=1}^N \left( {\partial S \over \partial n_i} \right)_{V,U,n_{j \neq j}} \cdot n_i
= S -{1 \over T} U + \sum_{i=1}^N {\mu_i \over T} n_i = \Psi_2 \! \left( V, {1 \over T}, {\mu \over T} \right)</math>
<math>Y = -{G \over T}</math>
<math>G = \sum_{i=1}^N \mu_i n_i</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y = - \sum_{i=1}^N n_i \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {\mu_i \over T} \right) - \sum_{i=1}^N {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y = -V \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T } \right) - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} {\mu_i \over T} \, \mathrm{d} n_i</math>
<math>U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right) + V \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T} \right) - \sum_{i=1}^{N} n_i \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {\mu_i \over T} \right) = 0</math>
<math>H \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right) + {V \over T} \, \mathrm{d} \! P - \sum_{i=1}^{N} n_i \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {\mu_i \over T} \right) = 0</math>
<math>H = U + PV</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} J = {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} V - U \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T } \right)</math>
<math>\left( {\partial J \over \partial {1 \over T}} \right)_{V,n} = -U</math>
<math>J = -{F \over T}</math>
<math>\left( {\partial {F \over T} \over \partial {1 \over T}} \right)_{V,n} = U</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} Y = -{V \over T} \, \mathrm{d} P - H \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right)</math>
<math>\left( {\partial Y \over \partial {1 \over T}} \right)_{P,n} = -H</math>
<math>Y = -{G \over T}</math>
<math>\left( {\partial {G \over T} \over \partial {1 \over T}} \right)_{P,n} = H</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} F = - P \, \mathrm{d} V - S \, \mathrm{d} T</math>
<math>\left( {\partial F \over \partial T} \right)_{V,n} = -S</math>
<math>\left( {\partial J \over \partial {1 \over T}} \right)_{V,n} = -U</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T} \right) = {\mathrm{d} P \over T} + P \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {1 \over T} \right)
= {\mathrm{d} P \over T} - {P \over T^2} \, \mathrm{d} T</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} P = T \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T} \right) + {P \over T} \, \mathrm{d} T</math>
<math>\mathrm{d} G = V \, \mathrm{d} P - S \, \mathrm{d} T
= VT \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T} \right) - \left( S - {P \over T} V \right) \, \mathrm{d} T
= VT \, \mathrm{d} \! \left( {P \over T} \right) - \Psi_1 \, \mathrm{d} T</math>
<math>\left( {\partial G \over \partial T} \right)_{{P \over T},n} = -\Psi_1</math>
<math>\left( {\partial Y \over \partial {1 \over T}} \right)_{P,n} = -H</math>
<math>\delta Q_V = C_V \, \mathrm{d} T = T \, \mathrm{d} S = \mathrm{d} U</math>
<math>{C_V \over T} = \left( {\partial S \over \partial T} \right)_{V,n}</math>
<math>C_V = \left( {\partial U \over \partial T} \right)_{V,n}
= \left( {\partial {1 \over T} \over \partial T} \right)_{V,n} \left( {\partial U \over \partial {1 \over T} } \right)_{V,n}
= -{1 \over T^2} \left( {\partial U \over \partial {1 \over T} } \right)_{V,n}</math>

<math>H = U + PV</math>

<title>Lemma di Jordan</title>
<math>0\leq\theta_1&lt;\theta_2\leq\pi</math>
<math> \lim_{R \rightarrow +\infty}\max_{\theta\in[\theta_1;\theta_2]}|f(Re^{i\theta})|=0,</math>
<math> \lim_{R \rightarrow +\infty} \int_{\gamma_R} f(z)e^{i\omega z} dz=0,</math>
<math>\max_{z\in\gamma_R}\left|f(z)\right|=M_R\Rightarrow\lim_{R\rightarrow+\infty}M_R=0</math>
<math>\gamma_R(t)=Re^{it}</math>
<math>0\leq\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq\int_{\theta_1}^{\theta_2}\left|f(Re^{it})e^{iRe^{it}}iR\right|dt\leq R\int_{\theta_1}^{\theta_2}\left|f(Re^{it})\right|\cdot\left|e^{i\omega Re^{it}}\right|dt\leq M_RR\int_{\theta_1}^{\theta_2}\left|e^{i\omega Re^{it}}\right|dt</math>
<math>\left|e^{i\omega Re^{it}}\right|=\left|e^{\omega Ri(\cos t+i\sin t)}\right|=\left|e^{\omega R(i\cos t-\sin t)}\right|\leq e^{-\omega R\sin t}</math>
<math>\left|e^{i\omega Re^{it}}\right|=\left|e^{\omega Ri(\cos t+i\sin t)}\right|=\left|e^{\omega R(i\cos t-\sin t)}\right|\leq e^{-\omega R\sin t}</math>
<math>0\leq\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq M_RR\int_{\theta_1}^{\theta_2}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt\leq M_RR\int_0^{\pi}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt=2M_RR\int_0^{\frac{\pi}{2}}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt</math>
<math>0\leq\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq M_RR\int_{\theta_1}^{\theta_2}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt\leq M_RR\int_0^{\pi}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt=2M_RR\int_0^{\frac{\pi}{2}}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt</math>
<math>g(t)=\sin t,\,t\in\bigg[0,\frac{\pi}{2}\bigg]</math>
<math>h(t)=\frac{2}{\pi}t,\,t\in\bigg[0,\frac{\pi}{2}\bigg]</math>
<math>0\leq\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq 2M_RR\int_0^{\frac{\pi}{2}}e^{-\omega R\frac{2}{\pi}t}dt=-2M_RR\left[e^{-\omega R\frac{2}{\pi}t}\right]_0^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\cdot\frac{\pi}{2\omega R}=-\frac{\pi}{\omega}M_R\left(e^{-\omega R}-1\right)</math>
<math>0\leq\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq 2M_RR\int_0^{\frac{\pi}{2}}e^{-\omega R\frac{2}{\pi}t}dt=-2M_RR\left[e^{-\omega R\frac{2}{\pi}t}\right]_0^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\cdot\frac{\pi}{2\omega R}=-\frac{\pi}{\omega}M_R\left(e^{-\omega R}-1\right)</math>
<math>0\leq\lim_{R\rightarrow+\infty}\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq\lim_{R\rightarrow+\infty}-\frac{\pi}{\omega}M_R\left(e^{-\omega R}-1\right)=0</math>
<math>0\leq\lim_{R\rightarrow+\infty}\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq\lim_{R\rightarrow+\infty}-\frac{\pi}{\omega}M_R\left(e^{-\omega R}-1\right)=0</math>

<math>0\leq\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq M_RR\int_{\pi}^{2\pi}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt=M_RR\int_{-\pi}^0e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt=2M_RR\int^0_{-\frac{\pi}{2}}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt\leq2M_RR\int_{-\frac{\pi}{2}}^0e^{\omega R}dt</math>
<math>0\leq\left|\int_{\gamma_R}f(z)e^{i\omega z}dz\right|\leq M_RR\int_{\pi}^{2\pi}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt=M_RR\int_{-\pi}^0e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt=2M_RR\int^0_{-\frac{\pi}{2}}e^{-\omega R\sin t}dt\leq2M_RR\int_{-\frac{\pi}{2}}^0e^{\omega R}dt</math>

<math>\mathbf{J}_\mathrm{drift}(\mathbf{x}) = \mu(\mathbf{x}) F(\mathbf{x}) \rho(\mathbf{x}) = -\rho(\mathbf{x}) \mu(\mathbf{x}) \nabla U(\mathbf{x}),</math>
<math>\mathbf{J}_\mathrm{diffusion}(\mathbf{x})=-D(\mathbf{x}) \nabla \rho(\mathbf{x}),</math>
<math>\mathbf{J}_\mathrm{drift} + \mathbf{J}_\mathrm{diffusion} = 0</math>
<math>\nabla\rho = \frac{\mathrm{d}\rho}{\mathrm{d} U} \nabla U.</math>
<math>0 = \mathbf{J}_\mathrm{drift} + \mathbf{J}_\mathrm{diffusion} = -\mu \rho \nabla U - D \nabla \rho = \left(-\mu \rho - D \frac{\mathrm{d}\rho}{\mathrm{d} U}\right)\nabla U.</math>
<math>D = -\mu \frac{\rho}{\frac{\mathrm{d}\rho}{\mathrm{d} U}}.</math>
<math>\rho(\mathbf{x}) = A e^{-\frac{U(\mathbf{x})}{k_B T}},</math>
<math>\frac{\mathrm{d}\rho}{\mathrm{d} U} = -\frac{1}{k_B T}\rho,</math>
<math>D = -\mu \frac{\rho}{\frac{\mathrm{d}\rho}{\mathrm{d} U}} = \mu k_B T,</math>

  X[x,y]= x-y'\dfrac{x'^2+y'^2}{x'y''-x''y'}\\[10pt]

<title>Coble-kruip</title>
<math> met [[Project:AWB|AWB]]</comment>
      <model>wikitext</model>
      <format>text/x-wiki</format>
      <text xml:space="preserve">'''Coble-kruip''' ([[Engels]]: ''Coble creep'') is een vorm van [[diffusiekruip]] in [[kristallijne stof]]fen (stoffen die opgebouwd zijn uit [[Kristal (natuurwetenschappen)|kristallen]], in de [[materiaalkunde]] ook wel [[korrel (kristal)|korrels]] genoemd), waarbij de [[diffusie]] van [[vacancy|vacancies]] aan de [[korrelgrens|korrelgrenzen]] plaatsvindt. Als de stof zich onder een [[differentiaalspanning]] bevindt leidt dit tot een stroom van deeltjes door de korrelgrenzen naar de vlakken van een korrel waar de kleinste [[compressie (geologie)|compressieve]] [[mechanische spanning|spanning]] op staat. Door deze stroming van deeltjes [[deformatie|deformeert]] de korrel.

Coble-kruip is genoemd naar [[Robert Coble]], een [[Verenigde Staten|Amerikaans]] [[materiaalkunde|materiaalkundige]] die in 1963 als eerste over deze vorm van [[kruip]] in materialen [[wetenschappelijke publicatie|publiceerde]].&lt;ref&gt;{{en}}{{aut|[[Robert Coble|Coble, R.L.]]}}; 1963: ''A Model for Boundary Diffusion Controlled Creep in Polycrystalline Materials'', Journal of Applied Physics '''34''', p. 1679.&lt;/ref&gt;

==Vervorming door Coble-kruip==
De snelheid van [[vervorming]] (Engels: ''strain rate'') van een materiaal wordt bij Coble-creep gegeven met de formule:

:&lt;math&gt;\dot{\epsilon} = \frac{\sigma}{d^3} D_C e^{-Q_{Coble}/RT}</math>
<math>\dot{\epsilon} = \frac{\sigma}{d^3} D_C e^{-Q_{Coble}/RT}</math>

<math>R = g^{ab} (\Gamma^c_{ab,c} - \Gamma^c_{ac,b} + \Gamma^d_{ab}\Gamma^c_{cd} - \Gamma^d_{ac} \Gamma^c_{bd})</math>

\sum_k \left(\sum_{i,j: i + j = k} a_i b_j\right)X^k.</math>

<title>Identidade de Euler</title>

<math>e^{ix} = \cos x + i \sin x</math>
<math>x = \pi</math>
<math>e^{i \pi} = \cos \pi + i \sin\pi</math>
<math>e^{i \pi} = -1</math>
<math>e^{i \pi} + 1 = 0</math>
<math>e^z = \sum_{n=0}^{\infty} \left ( \frac{z^n}{n!} \right ) = 1 + z + \frac{z^2}{2!} + \frac{z^3}{3!} \cdots</math>
<math>e^{z_1 + z_2} = e^{z_1} .e^{z_2}</math>
<math>z = iy \quad</math>
<math>e^{iy} = 1 + iy + \left ( \frac{(iy)^2}{2!} \right ) + \left ( \frac{(iy)^3}{3!} \right ) + \left ( \frac{(iy)^4}{4!} \right ) + \left ( \frac{(iy)^5}{5!} \right ) \cdots = 1 + iy - \left ( \frac{y^2}{2!} \right ) - i\left ( \frac{y^3}{3!} \right ) + \left ( \frac{y^4}{4!} \right ) + i\left ( \frac{y^5}{5!} \right ) \cdots</math>
<math> = 1 - \left ( \frac{y^2}{2!} \right ) + \left ( \frac{y^4}{4!} \right ) - \left ( \frac{y^6}{6!} \right ) \cdots + i( y - \left ( \frac{y^3}{3!} \right ) + \left ( \frac{y^5}{5!} \right ) \cdots) = \cos (y) + i \sin (y)</math>

<title>Coeficiente de variação</title>
<math>c_{\rm v}=\frac{\sigma}{\mu}.</math>
<math>0/100=0.</math>
<math>8,165/100=0,08165.</math>
<math>30,78/27,875=1,104.</math>
<math>\frac{4}{40}=0,1</math>
<math>\frac{4}{5}=0,8</math>
<math>15,81/20=0,79</math>
<math>28,46/68=0,42</math>
<math>\widehat{c_{\rm v}}=\frac{s}{\bar{x}}.</math>
<math>\widehat{c_{\rm v}}^*=\bigg(1+\frac{1}{4n}\bigg)\widehat{c_{\rm v}}.</math>
<math>\widehat{c_{\rm v}}_{\rm ln}= \sqrt{\mathrm{e}^{s_{\rm ln}^2}-1},</math>
<math>s_{\rm ln}=s_b\ln(b)</math>
<math>\mathrm{GCV_K}={\mathrm{e}^{s_{\rm ln}}-1}.</math>
<math>c_v(x)=c_v(\alpha x)</math>
<math>c_v(\{x,x\})=c_v(x)</math>
<math>\mathrm{d}F_{c_{\rm v}}=\frac{2}{\pi^{1/2} \Gamma \left(\frac{n-1}{2}\right)} \; \mathrm{e}^{-\frac{n}{2\left(\frac{\sigma}{\mu}\right)^2}\frac{{c_{\rm v}}^2}{1+{c_{\rm v}}^2}}\frac{{c_{\rm v}}^{n-2}}{(1+{c_{\rm v}}^2)^{n/2}}\sideset{}{^\prime}\sum_{i=0}^{n-1}\frac{(n-1)! \, \Gamma \left(\frac{n-i}{2}\right)}{(n-1-i)! \, i! \,}\frac{n^{i/2}}{2^{i/2} \left(\frac{\sigma}{\mu}\right)^i}\frac{1}{(1+{c_{\rm v}}^2)^{i/2}} \, \mathrm{d}c_{\rm v} ,</math>

<title>Regulador quadrático linear</title>
<math>\dot{x} = Ax + Bu</math>
<math>J = \int\limits_{0}^\infty \left( x^T Q x + u^T R u \right) dt</math>
<math>u = -R^{-1} B^T P x \,</math>
<math>A^T P + P A - P B R^{-1} B^T P + Q = 0 \,</math>
<math>x_{k+1} = A x_k + B u_k \,</math>
<math>J = \sum\limits_{k=0}^{\infty} \left( x_k^T Q x_k + u_k^T R u_k \right)</math>
<math>u_k = -F x_k \,</math>
<math>F = \tilde{R}^{-1} B^T P x_k \,</math>
<math>\tilde{R} = R + B^T P B</math>
<math>P = Q + A^T \left( P - P B \left( R + B^T P B \right)^{-1} B^T P \right) A</math>

<title>Escalar de curvatura de Ricci</title>
<math>R = -g^{\mu\nu}\left[\Gamma_{\mu\nu}^\lambda \Gamma_{\lambda\sigma}^\sigma -
\Gamma_{\mu\sigma}^\lambda \Gamma_{\nu\lambda}^\sigma \right]-\partial_\nu\left[g^{\mu\nu} \Gamma^\sigma_{\mu\sigma} -g^{\mu\sigma} \Gamma^\nu_{\mu\sigma} \right]</math>
<math>\Gamma^i_{kl}=\frac{1}{2}g^{im} \left(\frac{\partial g_{mk}}{\partial x^l} + \frac{\partial g_{ml}}{\partial x^k} - \frac{\partial g_{kl}}{\partial x^m} \right)</math>

<title>Equação de Pauli</title>
<math>\left[ \frac{1}{2m}(\vec{\sigma}\cdot(\vec{p} - q \vec{A}))^2 + q \phi \right] |\psi\rangle = i \hbar \frac{\partial}{\partial t} |\psi\rangle  </math>
<math> \begin{pmatrix} \psi_0 \\
\psi_1
\end{pmatrix} </math>
<math>\left[ \frac{1}{2m} \left( \sum_{n=1}^3 (\sigma_n ( - i \hbar \frac{\partial}{\partial x_n} - q A_n)) \right) ^2 + q \phi \right] 
\begin{pmatrix} \psi_0 \\ \psi_1 \end{pmatrix} 
= i \hbar \begin{pmatrix} \frac{ \partial \psi_0 }{\partial t} \\  \frac{ \partial \psi_1 }{\partial t}     \end{pmatrix}               </math>

<title>Série de Liouville-Neumann</title>
<math>\phi\left(x\right) = \sum^\infty_{n=0} \lambda^n \phi_n \left(x\right)</math>
<math>f(t)= \phi(t) - \lambda \int_a^bK(t,s)\phi(s)\,ds</math>
<math>K_n\left(x,z\right) = \int\int\cdots\int K\left(x,y_1\right)K\left(y_1,y_2\right) \cdots K\left(y_{n-1}, z\right) dy_1 dy_2 \cdots dy_{n-1}</math>
<math>\phi_n\left(x\right) = \int K_n\left(x,z\right)f\left(z\right)dz</math>
<math>K\left(x, z;\lambda\right) = \sum^\infty_{n=0} \lambda^n K_{n+1} \left(x, z\right)
</math>
<math>\phi\left(x\right) = \int K \left( x, z;\lambda\right) f\left(z\right)dz</math>

<title>Relação de Einstein (teoria cinética)</title>
<math> D = {{\mu_q \, k_B T}\over{q}}</math>
<math> D=\frac{k_B T}{6\pi\,\eta\,r} </math>
<math> D = \mu \, k_B T </math>
<math> D = \mu \, k_B T </math>
<math> D = \frac{\mu_q \, k_B T}{q} </math>
<math> \zeta = m\gamma = 6 \pi \, \eta \, r, </math>
<math> D=\frac{k_B T}{6\pi\,\eta\,r} </math>
<math> D = {{\mu_q \, p}\over{q  {{d \, p}\over{d \eta}}}} </math>
<math>F=-dU/dx</math>
<math>v=\mu F</math>
<math>J_\mathrm{deriva}(x) = \mu \, F(x) \, f(x) = -f(x) \mu \frac{dU}{dx}</math>
<math>J_\mathrm{difus.} (x)=-D \frac{df}{dx}</math>
<math>0 = J_\mathrm{deriva} + J_\mathrm{difus.} = -f(x) \mu \frac{dU}{dx} - D \frac{df}{dx} </math>
<math>f(x) = A e^{-U/(k_B T)}</math>
<math> \frac{df}{dx} = \frac{-dU/dx}{k_B T} f(x).</math>
<math>0 = J_\mathrm{deriva} + J_\mathrm{difus.} = -f(x) \mu \frac{dU}{dx} - D \frac{df}{dx} = -f(x)\frac{dU}{dx} \left(\mu-\frac{D}{k_B T}\right)</math>
<math>\mu=\frac{D}{k_B T}.</math>

<title>Lema de Jordan</title>
<math>C_R=\{z : z=R e^{i \theta}, \theta\in [0,\pi]\}</math>
<math> I_R = \int_{R} f(z) \ dz </math>
<math>f(z)=e^{iaz} g(z)\,,\quad z\in C_R,</math>
<math> \lim_{R \to \infty} I_R = 0 </math>
<math>\begin{align}
\int_{C_R} f(z)\, dz
&amp;=\int_0^\pi g(Re^{i\theta})\,e^{iaR(\cos\theta+i \sin\theta)}\,i Re^{i\theta}\,d\theta\\
&amp;=R\int_0^\pi g(Re^{i\theta})\,e^{aR(i\cos\theta-\sin\theta)}\,ie^{i\theta}\,d\theta\,.
\end{align}</math>
<math>\begin{align}
I_R:=\biggl|\int_{C_R} f(z)\, dz\biggr|
&amp;\le R\int_0^\pi\bigl|g(Re^{i\theta})\,e^{aR(i\cos\theta-\sin\theta)}\,ie^{i\theta} \bigr|\,d\theta\\
&amp;=R\int_0^\pi \bigl|g(Re^{i\theta})\bigr|\,e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta\,.
\end{align}</math>
<math>M_R:=\max_{\theta\in [0,\pi]} \bigl|g \bigl(R e^{i \theta}\bigr)\bigr| </math>
<math> I_R \le RM_R\int_0^\pi e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta = 2RM_R\int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-aR\sin\theta}\,d\theta\,.</math>
<math>M_R:=\max_{\theta\in [0,\pi]} \bigl|g \bigl(R e^{i \theta}\bigr)\bigr| \to 0\quad \mbox{quando } R \to \infty\,</math>
<math> I_R
\le 2RM_R \int_0^{\pi/2} e^{-2aR\theta/\pi}\,d\theta
=\frac{\pi}{a} (1-e^{-a R}) M_R\le\frac\pi{a}M_R\,.</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{1}{1+x^2}dx
</math>
<math>f(z)=\frac{1}{1+z^2}</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{1}{1+x^2}\,dx= \int_{-R}^R \frac{1}{1+x^2}\,dx + \int_{\Gamma_R} \frac{1}{1+z^2}\,dz = 2\pi i\,\operatorname{Res}(f,i)\,.</math>
<math> 2\pi i \operatorname{Res}(f,i)=2\pi i \lim_{z\to i}(z-i)f(z) = 2\pi i \lim_{z\to i}\frac{1}{z+i}= 2\pi i \frac{1}{2i}=\pi</math>
<math>\int_{-R}^R \frac{1}{1+x^2}\,dx + \int_{\Gamma_R} \frac{1}{1+z^2}\,dz = \pi </math>
<math> \lim_{R \to \infty}\left|  \frac{1}{1+z^2} \right| = 0 </math>
<math> \int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{1}{1+x^2}\,dx + 0 = 
\int_{-\infty}^\infty \frac{1}{1+x^2}\,dx = \pi </math>

<title>Combinatória enumerativa</title>
<math>F(x) = \sum^{\infty}_{n=0}f_nx^n</math>
<math>F(x) = \sum^{\infty}_{n=0}\frac{f_n}{n!}x^n</math>
<math>\mbox{Seq}(\mathcal{F}) = \epsilon\ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F} \ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F}\ \cup \cdots</math>
<math>1+F(x) + [F(x)]^2 + [F(x)]^3 + \cdots = \frac{1}{1-F(x)}</math>
<math>\mathcal{P} = \{\bullet\} \times \mbox{Seq}(\mathcal{P})</math>
<math>P(x) = x\frac{1}{1-P(x)}</math>
<math>P(x) = \frac{1-\sqrt{1-4x}}{2}</math>
<math>

\begin{align}

p_n &amp; = [x^n] P(x) = [x^n] \frac{1-\sqrt{1-4x}}{2} \\[6pt]

&amp; = [x^n] \frac{1}{2} - [x^n] \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{1-4x} \\[6pt]

&amp; = -\frac{1}{2} [x^n] \sum^{\infty}_{k=0} {\frac{1}{2} \choose k} (-4x)^k \\[6pt]

&amp; = -\frac{1}{2} {\frac{1}{2} \choose n} (-4)^n \\[6pt]

&amp; = \frac{1}{n} {2n-2 \choose n-1}

\end{align}

</math>

<title>Гауссова функция</title>
<math>g\left(x\right) = a e^{ -\frac{(x-b)^2}{2c^2} }</math>
<math>a = \frac{1}{\sigma\sqrt{2\pi}}</math>
<math>b = \mu</math>
<math>c = \sigma </math>
<math>b=0</math>
<math>w = 2 \sqrt{2 \ln 2}\ c \approx 2{,}35482 \cdot c</math>
<math>g(x) = a e^{- \frac{4 \ln (2) (x-b)^2 }{ w^2} }</math>
<math>x = b \pm c</math>
<math>\lim_{x\to\pm\infty}g(x) = 0</math>
<math>\int_{-\infty}^\infty a e^{- { (x-b)^2 \over 2 c^2 } }\,dx=ac\cdot\sqrt{2\pi}</math>
<math>a = \frac{1}{c\sqrt{2\pi}}</math>
<math>\mu = b</math>
<math>\sigma^2 = c^2</math>
<math>c^2 = c_1^2 + c_2^2</math>
<math>A = 1</math>
<math>(x_0, y_0) = (0, 0)</math>
<math>a = c = 1/2</math>
<math>b = 0</math>
<math>g(x,y) = A \cdot e^{\left(- \left(\frac{(x-x_0)^2}{2\sigma_x^2} + \frac{(y-y_0)^2}{2\sigma_y^2} \right)\right)}</math>
<math>V = \int_{-\infty}^\infty \int_{-\infty}^\infty g(x,y)\,dx \,dy=2 \pi A \sigma_x \sigma_y</math>
<math>g(x,y) = A \exp\left(- \left(a(x - x_0)^2 + 2b(x-x_0)(y-y_0) + c(y-y_0)^2 \right)\right)</math>
<math>g(x) = \exp(-x^TAx)</math>
<math>x= (x_1,\dots,x_n)</math>
<math> \int_{\R^n} \exp(-x^TAx) \, dx = \sqrt{\frac{\pi^n}{\det A}}</math>
<math>g(x) = \exp(-x^TAx+s^Tx)</math>
<math>s= (s_1,\dots,s_n)</math>
<math>A^T=A</math>
<math>sg(x) = A \exp\left(-\left(\frac{(x-x_o)^2}{2\sigma_x^2}\right)^P\right)</math>
<math>sg(x,y) = A \exp\left(- \left(\frac{(x-x_o)^2}{2\sigma_x^2}\right)^{P_x} - \left(\frac{(y-y_o)^2}{2\sigma_y^2} \right)^{P_y}\right)</math>

<title>Центрированное шестиугольное число</title>
<math>n^3 - (n-1)^3 = 3n(n-1)+1.</math>

<title>Уравнение состояния Ми — Грюнайзена</title>
<math>   p - p_0 = \frac{\Gamma}{V} (e - e_0), </math>
<math>\Gamma = V \left(\frac{dp}{de}\right)_V.</math>
<math>   \rho_0 U_s = \rho (U_s - U_p) ~~, \quad p_H - p_{H0} = \rho_0 U_s U_p ~~, \quad
   p_H U_p = \rho_0 U_s \left(\frac{U_p^2}{2} + E_H - E_{H0}\right), </math>
<math>
    \Gamma_0 = -\frac{1}{2d}\frac{\Pi'''(a)a^2 + (d-1)\left[\Pi''(a)a - \Pi'(a)\right]}{\Pi''(a)a + (d-1)\Pi'(a)},
</math>
<math> d=1 </math>
<math>d=2 </math>
<math>d=3 </math>
<math>d=\infty</math>

<title>Плотный граф</title>
<math>E = \frac {V (V-1)}{2}.</math>
<math>D = \frac{2E}{V\,(V-1)}</math>
<math>E = \frac {V (V-1)}{2},</math>

<title>Уравнение Пуассона — Больцмана</title>
<math>
\nabla\cdot\left[\varepsilon(\vec{r})\nabla\varphi(\vec{r})\right] = -\rho^{f}(\vec{r}) - \sum_{i}c_{i}^{\infty}z_{i} e_0  \exp \left[{\frac{-z_{i}e_0\varphi(\vec{r})}{k_{\rm B} T}}\right]
</math>

<title>Поточный алгоритм</title>
<math>\mathbf{a} = (a_1, \dots, a_n)</math>
<math>c = 1</math>
<math>F_k(\mathbf{a}) = \sum_{i=1}^n a_i^k</math>
<math>F_k(\mathbf{a}) = \sum_{i=1}^n
\frac{a_i}{m}\log{\frac{a_i}{m}}</math>
<math>m = \sum_{i=1}^n a_i</math>

<title>Уравнение Стейнхарта — Харта</title>
<math>{\frac 1{T}= \sum_{i=0}^{\infty} a_i \ln^i(R) =}</math>
<math>{= a_0 + a_1 \ln(R) + a_2 \ln^2(R) + a_3 \ln^3(R) + a_4 \ln^4(R) + \ldots}</math>
<math>{1 \over T} = A + B \ln(R) + C [\ln(R)]^3 ,</math>
<math>A = a_0,</math>
<math>B = a_1,</math>
<math>C = a_3.</math>
<math>R = \exp\left(\sqrt[3]{y - {x\over 2}} - \sqrt[3]{y + {x\over 2}}\right),</math>
<math>\begin{align}
  x &amp;= \frac{1}{C}\left(A - \frac{1}{T}\right), \\
  y &amp;= \sqrt{\left({B \over 3C}\right)^3 + \left(\frac{x}{2}\right)^2}.
\end{align}</math>
<math>\begin{bmatrix}
    1 &amp; \ln\left(R_1\right) &amp; \ln^3\left(R_1\right) \\
    1 &amp; \ln\left(R_2\right) &amp; \ln^3\left(R_2\right) \\
    1 &amp; \ln\left(R_3\right) &amp; \ln^3\left(R_3\right)
 \end{bmatrix}\begin{bmatrix}
    A \\
    B \\
    C
 \end{bmatrix} = \begin{bmatrix}
   \frac{1}{T_1} \\
   \frac{1}{T_2} \\
   \frac{1}{T_3}
 \end{bmatrix}
</math>
<math>\begin{align}
            L_1 &amp;= \ln\left(R_1\right),\; L_2 = \ln\left(R_2\right),\; L_3 = \ln\left(R_3\right) \\
            Y_1 &amp;= \frac{1}{T_1},\; Y_2 = \frac{1}{T_2},\; Y_3 = \frac{1}{T_3} \\
       \gamma_2 &amp;= \frac{Y_2 - Y_1}{L_2 - L_1},\; \gamma_3 = \frac{Y_3 - Y_1}{L_3 - L_1} \\
  \Rightarrow C &amp;= \left( \frac{ \gamma_3 - \gamma_2 }{ L_3 - L_2} \right) \left(L_1 + L_2 + L_3\right)^{-1} \\
  \Rightarrow B &amp;= \gamma_2 - C \left(L_1^2 + L_1 L_2 + L_2^2\right) \\
  \Rightarrow A &amp;= Y_1 - \left(B + L_1^2 C\right) L_1
\end{align}</math>

<title>Нелинейная регрессия</title>
<math> v = \frac{V_\max\ [\mbox{S}]}{K_m + [\mbox{S}]} </math>
<math> f(x,\boldsymbol\beta)= \frac{\beta_1 x}{\beta_2 + x} </math>
<math>J_{ij}=\frac{\partial f(x_i,\boldsymbol\beta)}{\partial \beta_j}</math>
<math> y = a e^{b x}U \,\!</math>
<math> \ln{(y)} = \ln{(a)} + b x + u, \,\!</math>
<math> \frac{1}{v} = \frac{1}{V_\max} + \frac{K_m}{V_{\max}[S]}</math>

<title>Z-оценка</title>
<math>f(z)=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2\pi}}\exp\left ( \frac{-z^2}{2} \right )</math>
<math>z={x- \bar{X} \over S_x}</math>
<math>z = \begin{cases} \frac{(y/M)^L-1)}{L\ S}, &amp; \text{если }L\neq0 \\ \frac{1}{S}ln(y/M), &amp; \text{ если }L=0 \end{cases}</math>

<title>Когомологии пучков</title>
<math>f^*=g^*: H^j(Y,A)\to H^j(X,A).</math>
<math>\mathcal U=\{U_\alpha\}</math>
<math>U_{\alpha_0\ldots\alpha_k}=U_{\alpha_0}\cap\ldots U_{\alpha_k}</math>

<math>\mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{i} \pi } + 1 = 0\,</math>

<math>\mathrm{e}^{x+\mathrm{i}y}:=\mathrm{e}^x(\cos y+\mathrm{i}\sin y)\,</math>
<math>f(x) = \frac{ \cos(x) + \mathrm{i} \cdot \sin(x) } { \mathrm{e}^{ \mathrm{i} x } }</math>
<math>\mathrm{e}^{ \mathrm{i} x } \cdot \mathrm{e}^{ -\mathrm{i} x } = \mathrm{e}^{ 0 } = 1</math>
<math>f(x)=1 \,</math>
<math>f'(x) = 0 \,</math>
<math>
\left[\mathrm{e}^{ \mathrm{i} x } \right]' = \mathrm{i} \cdot \mathrm{e}^{ \mathrm{i} x }
</math>
<math>=\frac{(-\sin x+\mathrm i\cdot\cos x)\cdot\mathrm e^{\mathrm ix}-(\cos x+\mathrm i\cdot\sin x)\cdot\mathrm i\cdot\mathrm e^{\mathrm ix}}{(\mathrm e^{\mathrm ix})^2}</math>
<math>=\frac{-\sin x\cdot\mathrm e^{\mathrm ix}+\mathrm i\cdot\cos x\cdot\mathrm e^{\mathrm ix}-\mathrm i\cdot\cos x\cdot\mathrm e^{\mathrm ix}-\mathrm i^2\cdot\sin x\cdot\mathrm e^{\mathrm ix}}{(\mathrm e^{\mathrm ix})^2}</math>
<math>=0\,</math>
<math>f'(x) = 0 \,</math>
<math>
f(0) = \frac{ \cos(0) + \mathrm{i} \cdot \sin(0)}{ \mathrm e^{\mathrm i0} } = \frac{ 1 + 0 }{ \mathrm e^{0} } = \frac{1}{1} = 1
</math>

</math>
<math>
\cos(x) = \sum_{k=0}^{N} (-1)^{k} \frac{ x^{2k} }{ (2k)! },\ \ \ \ N \rightarrow \infty
</math>
<math>
\sin(x) = \sum_{k=0}^{N} (-1)^{k} \frac{ x^{2k+1} }{ (2k+1)! },\ \ \ \ N \rightarrow \infty
</math>
<math>

    1 &amp; \ln\left(R_3\right) &amp; \ln\left(R_3\right)^3
 \end{bmatrix}\begin{bmatrix}
    A \\
    B \\
    C
 \end{bmatrix} = \begin{bmatrix}
   \frac{1}{T_1} \\
   \frac{1}{T_2} \\
   \frac{1}{T_3}
 \end{bmatrix}
</math>
<math>\begin{align}
            L_1 &amp;= \ln\left(R_1\right),\; L_2 = \ln\left(R_2\right),\; L_3 = \ln\left(R_3\right) \\
            Y_1 &amp;= \frac{1}{T_1},\; Y_2 = \frac{1}{T_2},\; Y_3 = \frac{1}{T_3} \\
       \gamma_2 &amp;= \frac{Y_2 - Y_1}{L_2 - L_1},\; \gamma_3 = \frac{Y_3 - Y_1}{L_3 - L_1} \\
  \Rightarrow C &amp;= \left( \frac{ \gamma_3 - \gamma_2 }{ L_3 - L_2} \right) \left(L_1 + L_2 + L_3\right)^{-1} \\
  \Rightarrow B &amp;= \gamma_2 - C \left(L_1^2 + L_1 L_2 + L_2^2\right) \\
  \Rightarrow A &amp;= Y_1 - \left(B + L_1^2 C\right) L_1
\end{align}</math>

<title>Нумераційна комбінаторика</title>
<math>F(x) = \sum^{\infty}_{n=0}f_nx^n</math>
<math>F(x) = \sum^{\infty}_{n=0}\frac{f_n}{n!}x^n</math>
<math>\mbox{Seq}(\mathcal{F}) = \epsilon\ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F} \ \cup\ \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F} \times \mathcal{F}\  \cup \cdots</math>
<math>1+F(x) + [F(x)]^2 + [F(x)]^3 + \cdots = \frac{1}{1-F(x)}</math>
<math>\mathcal{P} = \{\bullet\} \times \mbox{Seq}(\mathcal{P})</math>
<math>P(x) = x\frac{1}{1-P(x)}</math>
<math>P(x) = \frac{1-\sqrt{1-4x}}{2}</math>
<math>
\begin{align}
p_n &amp; = [x^n] P(x) = [x^n] \frac{1-\sqrt{1-4x}}{2} \\[6pt]
&amp; = [x^n] \frac{1}{2} - [x^n] \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{1-4x} \\[6pt]
&amp; = -\frac{1}{2} [x^n] \sum^{\infty}_{k=0} {\frac{1}{2} \choose k} (-4x)^k \\[6pt]
&amp; = -\frac{1}{2} {\frac{1}{2} \choose n} (-4)^n \\[6pt]
&amp; = \frac{1}{n} {2n-2 \choose n-1}
\end{align}
</math>

<math>\begin{bmatrix} dx \\ dy \end{bmatrix} = \begin{bmatrix} \frac{\partial x}{\partial r} &amp; \frac{\partial x}{\partial \theta} \\ \frac{\partial y}{\partial r} &amp; \frac{\partial y}{\partial \theta} \end{bmatrix}\begin{bmatrix} dr \\ d\theta \end{bmatrix} = \begin{bmatrix} \cos\theta &amp; -r\sin\theta \\ sin\theta &amp; r\cos\theta \end{bmatrix}\begin{bmatrix} dr \\ d\theta  \end{bmatrix} </math>
<math>J=\begin{bmatrix} \frac{\partial(x,y)}{\partial(r,\theta)} \end{bmatrix}</math>
<math>dxdy = \begin{bmatrix} \frac{\partial x}{\partial r} &amp; \frac{\partial x}{\partial \theta} \\ \frac{\partial y}{\partial r} &amp; \frac{\partial y}{\partial \theta} \end{bmatrix}drd\theta = rdrd\theta  </math>
<math>I^2=\int\limits_{-\infty}^{\infty}\int\limits_{-\infty}^{\infty}  e^{-x^2+y^2} dxdy = \int\limits_{0}^{2\pi}\int\limits_{0}^{\infty}  e^{-r^2} rdrd\theta</math>
<math>I^2= \int\limits_{0}^{2\pi}\int\limits_{0}^{\infty}  e^{-r^2} rdrd\theta = \int\limits_{0}^{2\pi} [  e^{-r^2}]_{0}^{\infty} drd\theta =  \int\limits_{0}^{2\pi} \frac{1}{2} d\theta = \pi </math>
<math>I=\sqrt\pi.</math>

<title>LQR控制器</title>
<math>\dot{x} = Ax + Bu</math>
<math>J =  x^T(t_1)F(t_1)x(t_1)  + \int\limits_{t_0}^{t_1} \left( x^T Q x + u^T R u + 2 x^T N u \right) dt</math>
<math>u = -K x \,</math>
<math>K = R^{-1} (B^T P(t) + N^T) \,</math>
<math>A^T P(t) + P(t) A - (P(t) B + N) R^{-1} (B^T P(t) + N^T) + Q = - \dot{P}(t) \,</math>
<math>P(t_1) = F(t_1).</math>
<math>\dot{x} = Ax + Bu</math>
<math>-\dot{\lambda} = Qx + Nu + A^T \lambda </math>
<math> 0 = Ru + N^Tx + B^T \lambda</math>
<math> x(t_0) = x_0</math>
<math> \lambda(t_1) = F(t_1) x(t_1)</math>
<math>\dot{x} = Ax + Bu</math>
<math>J = \int_{0}^\infty \left( x^T Q x + u^T R u + 2 x^T N u \right) dt</math>
<math>u = -K x \,</math>
<math>K = R^{-1} (B^T P + N^T) \,</math>
<math>A^T P + P A - (P B + N) R^{-1} (B^T P + N^T) + Q = 0 \,</math>
<math>\mathcal A^T P + P \mathcal A - P B R^{-1} B^T P + \mathcal Q = 0 \,</math>
<math>\mathcal A = A - B R^{-1} N^T \qquad  \mathcal Q = Q - N R^{-1} N^T \,</math>
<math>x_{k+1} = A x_k + B u_k \,</math>
<math>J = x_N^T Q x_N + \sum\limits_{k=0}^{N-1} \left( x_k^T Q x_k + u_k^T R u_k + 2 x_k^T N u_k \right)</math>
<math>u_k = -F_k x_{k} \,</math>
<math>F_k = (R + B^T P_{k+1} B)^{-1} (B^T P_{k+1} A + N^T) \,</math>
<math>P_{k-1} = A^T P_k A - (A^T P_k B + N) \left( R + B^T P_k B \right)^{-1} (B^T P_k A + N^T) + Q </math>
<math>P_N = Q</math>
<math>x_{k+1} = A x_k + B u_k \,</math>
<math>J = \sum\limits_{k=0}^{\infty} \left( x_k^T Q x_k + u_k^T R u_k + 2 x_k^T N u_k \right)</math>
<math>u_k = -F x_k \,</math>
<math>F = (R + B^T P B)^{-1} (B^T P A + N^T) \,</math>
<math>P = A^T P A - (A^T P B + N) \left( R + B^T P B \right)^{-1} (B^T P A + N^T) + Q </math>
<math>P = \mathcal A^T P \mathcal A - \mathcal A^T P B \left( R + B^T P B \right)^{-1} B^T P \mathcal A + \mathcal Q </math>
<math> \mathcal A = A - B R^{-1} N^T \qquad \mathcal Q = Q - N R^{-1} N^T </math>
